Essential Farms

The essential farms at each progression stage. Without them, progression stalls quickly.

📌 Priority Order

  • Priority 1: Wheat + chicken farm — basic food from the start
  • Priority 2: Blaze Farm — Blaze Rods needed very early (Eyes of Ender, potions)
  • Priority 3: Enderman Farm — massive XP for enchanting, Ender Pearls
  • Priority 4: Iron Farm — Iron Ingots for tools, armor, various crafts

🌱 Early Game — Foundations

Wheat / Carrot / Potato Farm

Vanilla

Basic farms with Farmer villagers who harvest automatically. The Farmer throws items into a chest — just collect. Supplement with Bonsai Trees for continuous wood.

  • Make a water farm for automatic harvesting
  • The Farmer villager harvests and replants alone
  • Bonsai Trees: 1-block tree that grows fast — perfect for wood

Passive Farm (Chickens / Cows / Sheep)

Vanilla

Enclosure with passive mobs. Chickens lay eggs (chance of chicken). Cows give leather and meat. Use Aquaculture for automated fishing too.

  • Chickens lay eggs — recycle into chickens via trapdoor floor
  • Aquaculture adds rare fish for recipes
  • Apple Cows give apples by hitting them — useful early

Zombie / Skeleton Farm

Vanilla

Trap a spawner in a dungeon. Make a water system to push mobs to a kill point. Collect drops (bones, gunpowder, etc.).

  • Do not destroy spawners — they are precious
  • Make a water system to centralize mobs
  • Bones → Bone Meal for farming

Blaze Farm

Vanilla (Fortress)

Find a Blaze Spawner in a Nether Fortress. Build a platform to attract Blazes then kill them. Blaze Rod = Blaze Powder = INDISPENSABLE for Eyes of Ender and potions.

  • Use a Blaze Spawner found in a Fortress
  • WitherSkeletonTweaks also helps obtain Wither Skeleton skulls
  • Place a water source just above to extinguish fire

⚙️ Mid Game — Automation

Spider Farm

Vanilla

Find a Spider Spawner. Very useful for String (webs) needed for bows and nets. String is also needed for decorative cobwebs and certain crafts.

  • String is needed for bows, nets, wool
  • The spider spawner can also be used for XP

Enderman Farm (Pre-End)

Vanilla

Build on a The End island after killing the Dragon. OR use an Enderman Spawner found in a structure. Massive XP source for enchanting your equipment.

  • Enderman XP is by far the best
  • Use a Pumpkin helmet to prevent them from attacking you
  • Collecting Ender Pearls for Eyes of Ender

Iron Farm

Vanilla

Build a village with enough villagers to trigger Iron Golem spawning. Killing them gives Iron. Requires at least 10 villagers and 10 beds (same number of beds as villagers).

  • More villagers = more Iron Golems spawned
  • Each Iron Golem gives 3-5 Iron Ingots
  • Automate with piston blades (Create)

Gold Farm (Nether)

Vanilla

In the Nether, Zombie Piglins drop Golden Swords/Ingots when killed after a delay. Very good XP/gold ratio. Use a Zombie Piglin spawner if found.

  • Zombie Piglins give gold after a delay
  • Very good for farming Gold quickly
  • Build in a Fortress to also get Wither Skeleton

Create Automation

Create

Create allows automating many things: conveyors to move items, mixers for recipes, shafts for mechanical power. Connect your farms with conveyors for a complete automated system.

  • Shaft + Cogwheel = power source for machines
  • Conveyor Belt moves items automatically
  • Mixer + Basin for bulk recipes
  • Deployer to place/collect automatically

Potion Farm

Vanilla

Automate potion production with automatic Brewers (Create or redstone). Regen and resistance potions are indispensable for bosses. Collect ingredients via appropriate farms.

  • Regen Potion = Ghast Tear + Blaze Powder
  • Fire Resistance Potion = Magma Cream + Blaze Powder
  • Spider Eye farm for Poison/Regen Potions

💎 Late Game — Optimization

Enderman Farm (The End)

Vanilla

On a The End island after the Dragon. The best spot for mass Enderman farming. Infinite XP for enchanting all your endgame armor and weapons.

  • Build an artificial island in a circle
  • Endermans fall from the floor to kill them
  • Most efficient XP source in the game

Chorus Farm

Vanilla

Chorus Fruit is needed for Chorus Flowers to plant. Harvest Chorus Plants with an automatic system. Useful for endgame crafts.

  • Chorus Plants grow vertically
  • Chorus Fruit is needed for certain crafts

Moa Farm (Aether)

The Aether

Moas are obtained by hatching a Moa Egg in a craftable Incubator. The hatched baby Moa follows you automatically. Raising Moas gives mass Feathers — useful for Elytra and flight.

  • Moas lay eggs after some time
  • Feathers are needed for vanilla Elytra
  • Protect Your Moa adds protection to your Moas

Dragon Egg Farm

Vanilla

Re-summon the Ender Dragon by placing 4 End Crystals on the 4 sides of the central Bedrock fountain. Each victory gives a Dragon Egg. Excellent for XP and eggs.

  • Re-summon: 4 End Crystals on the central Bedrock fountain (not the egg)
  • Each kill gives a new Dragon Egg
  • The Dragon Egg alone is not used for re-summoning

MineColonies — Automated Base

MineColonies

MineColonies allows creating a colony with citizens who work automatically. You can assign them roles (miner, farmer, cook) to automate your entire base.

  • The Miner digs automatically — passive resource source
  • The Farmer manages the fields
  • The Cook prepares food for citizens
  • The Builder constructs your buildings automatically

⚙️ Create — Complete Automation Guide

🔧 Core Create Concepts

  • Rotational Force (RF) : Create's energy — generated by water wheels, windmills, steam engines
  • Stress Units (SU) : Each machine consumes SU — calculate your production vs consumption
  • RPM (Rotations Per Minute) : Rotation speed — affects processing speed
  • Gear Ratios : Large cog (18 teeth) vs Small cog (6 teeth) = 3:1 ratio → 3× speed BUT 1/3 force
  • Overstressed : If SU consumed > SU generated, the entire system stops

💧 Energy Generation

  • Water Wheel : 3 wheels side by side in water flow = ~512 SU at 16 RPM
  • Windmill : 8× sails max, depends on wind (random), up to 1024 SU
  • Steam Engine : Late-game, fuel-based, 4096+ SU possible with boilers
  • Creative Motor : Creative only, infinite RPM and SU — test builds
  • Encased Fan + Lava : Alternative early game generation

🔗 Transmission & Control

  • Shafts : Transmit rotation, can be vertical/horizontal
  • Cogwheels : Change direction + gear ratios
  • Gearbox : Changes rotation direction 90°
  • Clutch : Start/stop transmission with redstone signal
  • Gearshift : Reverses rotation direction with redstone
  • Chain Drive : Transmits rotation without loss over long distance

🏭 Production Machines

  • Mechanical Press : Compress items (ingots → plates, etc.) — 8 SU
  • Mechanical Mixer : Mix items in basin — 32 SU, required for shapeless recipes
  • Mechanical Saw : Cut logs → planks (4×), stone → slabs — 4 SU
  • Millstone : Crush items (cobble → gravel → sand) — 4 SU
  • Encased Fan : Bulk washing, smelting, smoking — 2 SU per fan
  • Deployer : Simulates player interaction (place, break, use) — 4 SU

📦 Item Logistics

  • Mechanical Belt : Transports items horizontally — connects machines
  • Chute : Vertical transport (drop items down)
  • Smart Chute : Filterable, extracts items from containers
  • Funnel : Insert/extract items from inventories
  • Andesite Funnel : Basic, no filters
  • Brass Funnel : Filterable, precise control

🎯 Advanced Systems

  • Mechanical Arm : Transfers items between inventories (range 5 blocks)
  • Stockpile Switch : Emits redstone based on stored item quantity
  • Content Observer : Detects items on belt, emits redstone
  • Speed Controller : Precise RPM control with analog redstone
  • Rotation Speed Controller : Define exact RPM output

🚂 Mobile Contraptions

  • Mechanical Bearing : Rotate structures (windmills, drawbridges)
  • Mechanical Piston : Linear motion, extend/retract structures
  • Gantry : Move structures along a horizontal/vertical shaft
  • Cart Assembler : Transform minecarts into mobile contraptions
  • Linear Chassis : Connect blocks together for movement
  • Radial Chassis : Connect blocks in a radial shape

🏗️ Create Build Examples

  • Automatic Wheat Farm: Mechanical Plow (plants) + Mechanical Harvester (harvests) on Gantry + Mechanical Arm (storage)
  • Ore Processing 2×: Crusher → 2 raw ore → Fan (washing) → 2 nuggets + byproduct → Smelter → 2.5 ingots total
  • Auto-Crafter: Deployers placed around a Depot, automates the crafting sequence
  • Item Sorter: Belts + filtered Funnels = automatic item sorting
  • Mob Farm Auto-Kill: Deployers with swords on belt that mobs pass through
  • Tree Farm: Horizontal Mechanical Saw + Chassis = cuts entire tree, Deployers replant

⚙️ Extended Cogwheels — Additional Ratios

  • Half Cogwheel : Ratio 1:2 (half speed, double force)
  • Shiftable Cogwheel : Changes ratio with redstone
  • Clutched Cogwheel : Combines clutch and cogwheel in 1 block
  • Worm Gear : Extreme ratio 1:4 (very slow, very strong)
  • Compatible with base Create — extends possibilities

🏘️ MineColonies — Colony from A to Z

🏗️ Colony Start — First Steps

  • Supply Camp / Supply Ship : Starter structure (craft Supply Camp or Ship), place = colony start
  • Town Hall : Colony center — MUST be built first
  • Builder's Hut : Recruits the Builder — only he can build other buildings
  • Citizen Huts : Each citizen needs a bed in a hut
  • Happiness: Monitor morale — decent houses, varied food, security

🏛️ Essential Buildings (Order)

  • 1. Builder's Hut : Builds everything — absolute priority
  • 2. Citizen Huts ×4 : Housing for citizens (max 1 per hut)
  • 3. Deliveryman's Hut : Transports resources between buildings
  • 4. Restaurant/Bakery : Automatic food for citizens
  • 5. Warehouse : Central storage — couriers deposit here
  • 6. Mine : Passive resources (miner digs automatically)

🛠️ Production Buildings

  • Farm : Farmer cultivates crops (wheat, carrots, potatoes)
  • Lumberjack : Cuts trees, replants automatically
  • Miner : Digs mineshafts, brings up ores
  • Forester : Plants trees, manages forest
  • Fisher : Fishes (needs nearby water)
  • Composter : Transforms organic items → compost → dirt

⚔️ Defense & Security

  • Guard Tower : Guards patrol, defend against raids
  • Barracks : Barracks — multiple guards, upgradable
  • Archery : Trains archer guards (best ranged DPS)
  • Combat Academy : Trains knight guards (melee tank)
  • ⚠️ Raids: More citizens = stronger raids — defense is essential

🎓 Research & Upgrades

  • University: Unlocks research (speed, efficiency, capacity)
  • Library: Source of "knowledge" for the university
  • Priority research: Block Breaks (miner), Recipes (crafter), Citizen Skills
  • Levels : Citizens gain XP → level up → better efficiency
  • Tool Upgrades : Give better tools = faster production

🏪 Trade & Services

  • Tavern: Attracts visitors with quests and trades
  • Hospital : Heals injured citizens (after raids)
  • Stonemason : Produces stone bricks and variants
  • Sawmill : Transforms logs into planks in bulk
  • Fletcher : Crafts bows and arrows for guards
  • Blacksmith : Crafts tools and weapons for colony

📈 Advanced Optimization

  • Builder priorities: Right-click Town Hall → Work Orders → reorganize
  • Courier system : Multiple couriers = faster logistics
  • Auto-supply : Builder requests resources from warehouse automatically
  • Citizen assignment : Better stats = better jobs (check with scan tool)
  • Breeding program : Citizens with good traits → children with better stats

⚠️ Common Issues & Solutions

  • Builder stuck : Check that he has all materials (right-click hut → resources)
  • Citizens unhappy: Build better houses, diversify food, add decorations
  • Raids too hard: Increase number of guards, give them better equipment
  • Slow production: Level up workers, give them better tools, research upgrades
  • Not enough citizens: Build more citizen huts, increase happiness (natural reproduction)

🎯 MineColonies End-Game Strategies

  • Multiple Miners : 4-5 miners = massive passive ore income
  • Auto-Farming : Farmers + Restaurant/Bakery = infinite food for you too
  • Defense Grid : Guard Towers every 50 blocks = complete protection
  • Research maxed : University T5 = all buildings ultra-efficient
  • Create Integration: Warehouse → Create belts → Processing → Return to warehouse

Equipment Progression

How to upgrade your armor, weapons and passive items at each stage. Do not skip steps — you will die.

⚔️ Phase 1 — Early Game · Iron & Diamond

🪖 Armor

Vanilla → Witherite Armor

Quickly progress from iron to diamond. Witherite Armor (post-Wither Skeletons) bridges the gap before Netherite.

  • Iron: craft as soon as you get your first ores — essential protection
  • Diamond: 24 diamonds for a full set — absolute priority
  • Witherite: drops from Wither Skeletons, stats between Diamond and Netherite
  • Priority enchants: Protection I–II, Unbreaking II

⚔️ Weapons

Vanilla · Expanded Combat

Enchanted sword and bow to handle the first bosses. The shield (Expanded Combat) is essential from the iron phase.

  • Diamond Sword: Sharpness III minimum, Looting II recommended
  • Bow: Power IV, Punch II, Flame — 1 infinite arrow with Infinity
  • Shield: Expanded Combat improves blocking — always in the off-hand
  • Trident: Better Tridents makes the trident craftable early on

💍 Passive Slots (Curios)

Curios · Artifacts · Rings of Ascension

Open the Curios tab from the start — these slots offer permanent bonuses with no inventory cost.

  • Ring of Ascension: reduces fall damage — essential in the Aether
  • Artifacts: search dungeon chests as soon as possible
  • Void Totem: craft before going to The End — instant death otherwise
  • Inventory Totem: auto-activates on death from the inventory

🌙 Phase 2 — Mid Game · Diamond & Netherite

🪖 Armor

Vanilla · Caelus

Netherite via Smithing Table. 4 Ancient Debris at Y=15 → 4 Scraps → 1 Netherite Ingot + 4 Gold. Repeat for each piece.

  • Netherite: smelted in furnace, each piece requires 1 Ingot
  • Priority enchants: Protection IV, Unbreaking III, Mending on everything
  • Caelus: equip the Elytra (End Ship loot) WITHOUT losing your armor
  • Quality Equipment: prefer Rare/Epic drops — sometimes surpass crude Netherite

⚔️ Weapons

Soulslike Weaponry · More Bows & Arrows

Soulslike Weaponry unlocks 80+ weapons with unique Arts. Each weapon has a special skill activated by Sneak + Right-Click.

  • Soulslike : Claymore (Perseverance), Moonlight GS (lunar rays), Dragon Slayer GS (AoE)
  • More Bows: Longbow (+50% damage), Frost Bow (slows), Explosive Arrows (AoE)
  • Dreadsteel: available after killing Stage 5 Ice & Fire Dragon — surpasses Netherite
  • Weapon Arts: scale with Strength / Dexterity (Puffish Attributes)

💍 Passive Slots (Curios)

Artifacts · Rings of Ascension · Caelus

Multiplying Curios slots is now critical. Each active slot gives a permanent combat advantage.

  • Elytra (Caelus): separate flight slot from armor — game-changer for exploration
  • Artifacts rares : Running Shoes (speed), Mimic's Tooth (double-jump), Umbrella (glide)
  • Ring of Regeneration: constant passive regeneration — compensates for lack of healer
  • Ring of Flight: passive flight — only obtainable as a drop

🏆 Phase 3 — Boss Gear · Dimensional Armor

🪖 Boss Armor

TF · The Aether · Ice & Fire · Witherite Armor

Each major dimension drops a thematic armor with unique bonuses. Collect them before facing the Cataclysm bosses.

  • Twilight Dragon Armor : post-TF Dragon — best defense pre-enchanted Netherite
  • Valkyrie Armor : Valkyrie Queen drop (Aether) — aerial mobility bonus
  • Ice & Fire Dragon Armor: elemental resistance based on dragon type (fire / ice / lightning)
  • Armor of the Ages : historical sets (Samurai, Legionnaire, Knight) — unique bonuses per set

⚔️ Boss Weapons

Dreadsteel · Ice & Fire · Soulslike Weaponry

Dreadsteel is the key intermediate step between Netherite and Cataclysm. Obtained only from Stage 5 dragons.

  • Dreadsteel Sword: massive damage + elemental effect depending on dragon killed
  • Dreadsteel Armor: built-in elemental resistances — ideal against dimensional bosses
  • Soul Rend (Dreadsteel enchant): reduces enemy magic and fire resistances
  • Dread Strike: each hit reduces enemy resistance by 20% — up to 3 stacks

💍 Passive Slots (Curios)

Cataclysm Artifacts · Rings of Ascension · Artifacts

Fill all available Curios slots with the best found Artifacts. Each slot is a permanent passive advantage.

  • Witherite Armor: Wither Effect resistance bonus — essential in the Nether and against the Wither Boss
  • Specialized enchants: Dragon Slayer V (swords/axes), Dragon Protection IV (armors)
  • Execution (Scaling Health): bonus damage proportional to missing HP — perfect for finishing off bosses
  • Easy Magic: reroll enchantments without losing existing ones — optimize before boss fights

💀 Phase 4 — Endgame · The Cataclysm Universe

🪖 Armor Endgame

L'Ender's Cataclysm · Cataclysm Weaponry

Cataclysm armor is the maximum defense in the modpack. Craftable only with materials dropped by Cataclysm bosses.

  • Cataclysm Armor: maximum DEF + built-in Void resistances
  • Void Resistance (enchant): massively reduces damage from rank 5 Cataclysm bosses
  • Dread Shield (enchant Dreadsteel) : temporary shield at 30% HP — 60s cooldown
  • ⚠️ Prerequisite: defeat the Eyeless Lord to obtain the first Cataclysm materials

⚔️ Arsenal Endgame

Cataclysm Weaponry 2.0 · Cataclysm Tools · Soulslike Weaponry

CataclysmWeaponery 2.0 contains the most powerful weapons in the modpack. Each requires at least 1 Cataclysm boss for materials.

  • Ignis: flaming sword with fire trail — Inferno Slash enchant for AoE
  • Runic Blade: magic damage + active runes — Dark Edge partially ignores armor
  • Cataclysm Tools : pickaxe/axe/shovel post-Cataclysm — 2× speed vs Netherite, 4000+ durability
  • Soul Edge (Soulslike): AoE energy wave in a 5-block radius after each kill — perfect in groups

💍 Passive Slots (Curios)

Cataclysm Artifacts · Rings of Ascension · Artifacts

5 Cataclysm Artifacts equippable simultaneously. Each is an exclusive Cataclysm boss drop — not craftable.

  • Soul Render Fragment: +15% damage to all bosses (Eyeless Lord drop)
  • Ignitium Heart: regenerates 1 heart every 30s in combat (The Furnace drop)
  • Void Eye: see through walls within a 10-block radius (The Remnant drop)
  • Rings of Ascension Grade 5 : hands-free free flight — the best endgame transport

💎 Equipment Tips — Optimization

  • Enderman Farm first: build the XP farm in The End BEFORE enchanting — hundreds of levels are needed to enchant all endgame gear.
  • Easy Magic + Disenchanting Table: reroll bad enchantments, recover good ones from looted items — never waste a Mending or Sharpness V.
  • Curios — all slots: hat, amulet, ring ×2, belt, Curios boots — each slot is a passive bonus. Aim for 5+ active slots from Phase 2 onward.
  • Caelus: equipping the Elytra in the Caelus slot keeps full armor — essential for flying without sacrificing defense.
  • Quality Equipment: mob drops have a random quality (Crude → Epic). A well-enchanted Rare can surpass a Netherite Crude — always check the stars.
  • Scaling Health: killing mobs regularly increases your max health passively — bosses are also much stronger in multiplayer, adjust your equipment accordingly.

🔨 Key Crafts & Recipes

⚔️ Essential Weapons

  • Enchanted Diamond Sword: Sharpness III minimum, Looting II recommended
  • Bow + Infinity : Power IV, Punch II, Flame — 1 arrow = infinite
  • Trident (Better Tridents) : Craftable with Prismarine + Nautilus Shell
  • Soulslike Weaponry : Check JEI for recipes (boss materials required)
  • CataclysmWeaponery : Only after the Eyeless Lord

🛡️ Armor Progression

  • Iron → Diamond: Craft full set at 24 diamonds
  • Netherite Upgrade: Smithing Table + Netherite Ingot per piece (smelt 4 Ancient Debris = 4 Netherite Scraps → 4 Scraps + 4 Gold = 1 Netherite Ingot)
  • Priority enchants: Protection IV, Unbreaking III, Mending
  • Specialized Armor : Fire Protection for Nether, Blast Protection for Creepers
  • Twilight Dragon Armor : Post-TF Dragon, best defense pre-Netherite

🧪 Essential Potions

  • Fire Resistance II: Magma Cream + Redstone (8 min) — MANDATORY Nether
  • Regeneration II: Ghast Tear + Glowstone — boss combat
  • Strength II: Blaze Powder + Glowstone — +260% damage
  • Speed II: Sugar + Glowstone — boss dodging
  • Night Vision: Golden Carrot — cave/Nether exploration
  • Turtle Master: Turtle Shell — +60% damage reduction, -60% speed

🍎 Food & Buffs

  • Golden Apple: 8 Gold Ingots + Apple — Regen II + Absorption
  • Enchanted Golden Apple: Found only (loot), save for boss
  • Honey Bottle: Cures Poison — always have 3+

🔮 Magic Items & Artifacts

  • Ender Chest: 8 Obsidian + Eye of Ender — global inventory
  • Shulker Box: Post-End, portable chest — 27 slots
  • Elytra: End Ship loot — activate Caelus for separate slot
  • Totem of Undying: Evoker drop (Mansion/Raid) — cheat death
  • Void Totem: Craft — see JEI — mandatory Void survival

⚙️ Special Tools

  • Pickaxe Fortune III: +120% ores (diamonds, emeralds)
  • Silk Touch Pickaxe: Collect spawners, ice
  • Shears: Sheep, leaves, cobwebs — efficiency +500%
  • Bucket: Water = obsidian farming, lava = infinite fuel
  • Flint & Steel: Portals, clearing mobs, lighting campfires

🏗️ Utility Blocks

  • Crafting Table : Always 3+ in exploration inventory
  • Furnace: Blast Furnace (2× faster ores), Smoker (2× faster food)
  • Anvil: Repair + enchant — XP level required
  • Enchanting Table: 15 bookshelves = max level 30
  • Brewing Stand: Blaze Rod required — automate with Create
  • Smithing Table: Netherite upgrade + Armor Trim

🎒 Mobile Storage

  • Useful Backpacks: Backpacks in multiple sizes (Small → Huge, 9 to 54 slots), equippable via Curios slots
  • Shulker Boxes: 27 portable slots post-End
  • Ender Chest: Global inventory access — place in base
  • Bundle (vanilla): Group varied items in 1 slot
  • Useful Backpacks:

💎 Ores — Optimal Layers

  • Diamonds: Y=-59 to Y=-64 (deepslate) — branch mining recommended
  • Ancient Debris (Netherite): Y=15 (best) or Y=8-22 — bed mining dangerous but effective
  • Emeralds: Mountains only, Y=224-256 — very rare
  • Lapis: Y=0 (peak) — useful for enchantments
  • Redstone: Y=-59 to Y=-64 — Create automation
  • Iron: Y=16 and Y=232 (two peaks) — most abundant
  • Gold: Badlands Y=256 (peak) or Nether Y=15
  • Copper: Y=48 (peak) — Lightning Rod, Spyglass, Create

Solo / Duo / Trio+

Scaling Health makes mobs more powerful in multiplayer. Here's how to adapt your strategy based on player count.

⚠️ How Scaling Health Works

  • Each additional player increases mob HP AND damage within a 256-block radius
  • Solo: bosses are at their base power
  • Duo: approximately +40-60% HP and damage on bosses
  • Trio+: each additional player adds even more — bosses become formidable
  • Scaling also applies to regular mobs — even Creepers are more dangerous in groups
Boss Solo Duo Trio+
Blaze LordAccessible in iron/diamond. Fire potions mandatory. Bow recommended.Doable One in melee, one with bow. Share potions.Easy One tank, one DPS, one healer. Blaze Lord is manageable.
The WitherUnderwater bunker mandatory. Many heals. Sword + shield.Doable One destroys the skulls in phase 2, the other attacks. More healing needed.Difficult The Wither is much stronger in trio. Strict roles: one per skull, one on the body.
Ender DragonDestroy the crystals then attack when the head lands. Many arrows.Doable One on the crystals, one in melee. Much faster.Easy Two on the crystals, one in melee. Kill quickly before scaling ramps up.
SliderKeep moving on the small platform. Watch out for shell explosions.Easy Both attack the shells. More DPS = shorter fight.Easy Very fast in groups. The platform is small — coordination needed.
The LichDestroy the 4 Jars then attack. Managing skeletons alone is hard.Doable One on the Jars, one handles the skeletons. Much more manageable.Difficult There are far more skeletons. Having a healer is essential.
The HydraVery difficult solo — the heads overwhelm. Attack the body only.Doable One per side to cover the heads. Much more manageable.Difficult The Hydra is ENORMOUS in trio+. One per side + one healer recommended.
Dragons (I&F)Very hard at Stage 4-5 solo. Requires perfect equipment.Doable One draws the Dragon, the other attacks. Effective attack rotation.Difficult Stage 5 Dragons in trio+ are monsters. Endgame equipment mandatory.
Eyeless LordVery hard — she is extremely fast. CataclysmWeaponery mandatory.Doable In duo she is stronger but you can take turns.Very Hard She is formidable in trio+. Perfect coordination needed.
The CataclysmNearly impossible solo without perfect equipment.Difficult Doable but very hard. Both players must be in endgame gear.Very Hard THE hardest fight in the modpack in trio+. Strict roles mandatory: Tank / DPS / Healer.
Mother of MowziesNearly impossible — she summons multiple bosses simultaneously.Difficult Each player handles a servant. Coordination essential.Doable In trio: one player per summoned servant. Much more manageable.
Giant BumblezoidBuild a barricade beforehand. Minions overwhelm quickly in solo.Doable One on the minions, one on the Giant.Easy Minions are quickly handled in groups.

🗡️ Solo — The Self-Sufficient

Solo Strategy

In solo, you are your own tank, DPS and healer. Bosses at base power — more accessible. Prepare a lot of healing before each boss. Build protection structures (walls, barricades) before fights. Stock up on potions in large quantities before entering.

  • Always have 32+ Golden Apples on you
  • Build a wall before boss fights
  • Master potions — Regen III is your best friend
  • Passive Artifacts (health, regen) are essential

🛡️ Duo — The Partnership

Duo Strategy

In duo, you can split roles: one Tank (heavy armor, shield) and a DPS (bow or fast sword). The Tank draws boss aggro, the DPS deals damage. You can also take turns healing each other.

  • Tank role: heavy armor + shield + regen potions
  • DPS role: bow (ranged) or fast sword (melee)
  • The Tank applies poisons/status effects on the boss
  • Take turns: when one is hurt, the other takes focus

⚔️ Trio+ — The Brigade

Trio+ Strategy

In trio or more, roles become even more specialized. Scaling is very high — you MUST organize. Tank absorbs hits, DPS deals damage, Healer distributes healing and handles minions.

  • Tank: maximum armor + shield + permanent Regen
  • DPS: most powerful weapons, focus on the boss
  • Healer: healing potions, manage minions, revive
  • Communication essential — announce attacks

🏘️ General Multiplayer Tips

  • FTB Chunks: Protect your base with claimed chunks — other players cannot touch your blocks.
  • Share farms: Each player should not have their own farms. Create shared farms and specialize.
  • Logistics: Name your chests, build central warehouses. JEI is your best friend for finding what goes where.
  • Waystones: Place Waystones outside boss rooms — you can return quickly after a death.
  • Tombstone: The Tombstone mod places a grave at your death with your items — you will never lose your items.

Modpack Systems

The progression, survival and utility systems added by mods. Understanding these systems is key to the modpack.

⚗️ Dragon Finder & Dragon Seeker

Dragon Finder / Dragon Seeker

Two complementary tools to locate Ice & Fire dragons. Dragon Finder = compass pointing to the nearest dragon nest. Dragon Seeker = displays dragon positions on the JourneyMap.

  • Craft Dragon Finder with dragon scales
  • Check the biome before searching: Fire = volcanoes, Ice = mountains
  • Dragon Seeker adds automatic markers on JourneyMap
  • Essential for finding Stage 1 eggs to tame

⚔️ Dreadsteel

Dreadsteel

Legendary material obtained only by killing Stage 5 Ice & Fire dragons. Allows forging weapons and armors that surpass Netherite in damage and durability.

  • Required: kill a Stage 5 Dragon (Fire, Ice or Lightning)
  • Dreadsteel Sword: massive damage + elemental effect based on dragon type
  • Dreadsteel Armor: built-in elemental resistances
  • Intermediate step BEFORE Cataclysm weapons

🏆 Quality Equipment

Quality Equipment

Quality system on all equipment. Items drop with a random rarity that influences their stats: damage, durability, speed.

  • Levels: Crude → Common → Uncommon → Rare → Epic
  • A Rare can surpass crude Netherite
  • Farm bosses to obtain Epic drops
  • Compatible with Soulslike Weaponry and other mod weapons

🛡️ Expanded Combat

Expanded Combat

Improved combat system. New attack animations, combos, dodge rolls, counter-attacks. Makes combat more dynamic.

  • Roll: double-tap direction to dodge
  • Combo: chaining attacks increases damage
  • Counter: blocking at the right moment = staggers the enemy
  • Works with all weapons in the modpack

💍 Artifacts

Artifacts

Special items found in dungeons and rare chests. Each gives a unique bonus when equipped in Curios slots. Enormous variety of powers.

  • Umbrella : protection pluie + glide en descendant
  • Running Shoes : vitesse augmentée significativement
  • Mimic's Tooth: double-jump
  • Pocket Piston: increased knockback on attacks
  • Always check dungeon chests for rare artifacts

🗡️ Witherite Armor

Witherite Armor

Armor crafted with Witherite (material obtained from Wither Skeletons). Solid alternative between Diamond and Netherite, accessible earlier in the progression.

  • Craft: Witherite Ingots (from Wither Skeleton drops)
  • Stats: between Diamond and Netherite
  • Bonus: Wither Effect resistance
  • Ideal for the pre-Netherite phase

🏰 Dungeons & Taverns

Dungeons & Taverns

Complete rework of vanilla structures. Taverns in villages, reinforced dungeons, massive Pillager outposts, redesigned strongholds, Ancient City overhaul.

  • Taverns: merchants with unique trades, rest
  • Strongholds: much larger, more rooms
  • Pillager Outposts: imposing towers, patrolling guards
  • Ancient City: even more dangerous and richly looted

🏛️ Dungeon Crawl

Dungeon Crawl

Multi-level procedural dungeons that go deep underground. Each floor is harder and better looted. Final boss at the deepest level.

  • Enter via a spiral staircase on the surface
  • Up to 8+ levels going down
  • Loot progressively improves per level
  • Final boss = chest with guaranteed endgame loot
  • Use the JourneyMap minimap to map your route

⛏️ FTB Ultimine

FTB Ultimine

Built-in vein mining. Hold the ~ key and mining one block extracts the entire vein automatically. Revolutionizes ore mining.

  • Activate: hold ~ key + mine the first ore block
  • Works on all ores and trees
  • Configurable block limit per vein mine
  • Saves hours of repetitive mining
  • Fortune/Silk Touch applied to the entire vein

🛡️ Tombstone

Tombstone

Upon death, a grave is generated with all your items inside. The grave has an associated key that appears in your inventory on respawn. Items are protected from despawning.

  • Key appears in your inventory after respawn
  • The grave is indestructible without the key
  • Items NEVER despawn inside the grave
  • Use Waystones to find the grave easily
  • Config: enable "back to life" to teleport back to the grave

🎮 Puffish Skills

Puffish Skills + Puffish Attributes

RPG skill tree system. With each level up (XP), you gain a skill point. Different trees for combat, magic, exploration, etc. Skills progressively improve your stats.

  • Invest first in Health and Regen — surviving is the priority
  • Combat skills are essential before boss fights
  • Exploration adds useful abilities (night vision, etc.)
  • Puffish Attributes adds additional customizable attributes

❤️ Scaling Health

Scaling Health

Your maximum health increases with each mob killed. The more you explore and fight, the higher your health goes. In multiplayer, mobs also gain health and deal more damage for each additional player in range.

  • Killing mobs regularly increases your max health
  • In multiplayer: bosses are MUCH stronger
  • Build farms = passively increase your health
  • Use Max Health Fix to avoid max health bugs

💎 Curios

Curios

Adds additional equipment slots on your character: hat, amulet, ring, belt, extra boots. You can equip Artifacts, Rings of Ascension and other passive items in these slots.

  • Open the Curios tab in your inventory
  • Rings of Ascension go in the Ring slot
  • Artifacts are placed in their appropriate slots
  • Each slot adds important passive bonuses

🪂 Caelus

Caelus

Allows equipping Elytra AT THE SAME TIME as your armor in a separate slot. Normally, Elytra replaces the chestplate in your armor. With Caelus, you keep your full armor AND you fly.

  • Game-changer: full armor + flight simultaneously
  • Elytra goes in the Caelus slot (Curios tab)
  • Rockets for Elytra work as usual
  • Perfect for late-game where you explore while flying everywhere

⚰️ Tombstone

Tombstone

When you die, a grave appears at your death point with all your items. You can go back and retrieve your belongings instead of losing them in the void or an inaccessible place.

  • Your items are ALWAYS saved on death
  • The grave has a timer — get there before it disappears
  • In multiplayer: a teammate can retrieve your items
  • You can configure the grave's lifespan

🕳️ Void Totem

Void Totem

A totem that saves you from falling into the Void (mainly The End). Without it, falling into the Void = instant death and loss of all your items. ALWAYS have one on you in The End.

  • MANDATORY in The End — always have one in your hotbar
  • It is consumed on each use — craft several
  • You respawn at the End portal after activation

📦 Inventory Totem

Inventory Totem

Similar to the Void Totem but to protect your inventory on death in general. Can be configured to keep certain items even on death.

  • Configurable — choose which items are protected
  • Combines well with Tombstone
  • Very useful for dangerous explorations

💍 Rings of Ascension

Rings of Ascension

Power rings equippable in Curios slots. Each ring gives a powerful bonus: flight, speed, regen, resistance. High-grade rings are extremely powerful but very hard to obtain.

  • Rings go in the Ring slots (Curios)
  • Grade 1 = weak bonus, Grade 5 = massive bonus
  • The Ring of Flight enables passive flight
  • Find in structures or buy from rare villagers

✨ Artifacts

Artifacts

Passive items equippable via Curios. Each gives a unique bonus: regen, resistance, attack, etc. Found in structures and dungeons. Combine multiple Artifacts for massive bonuses.

  • Artifacts go in the appropriate Curios slots
  • Some Artifacts stack — equip multiple of them
  • Search in dungeons (Dungeon Crawl, Dungeons Plus)
  • Cataclysm Artifacts are the best in endgame

🏅 Quality Equipment

Quality Equipment

Items dropped by mobs have a random "quality" (1-5 stars). Quality affects item stats — 4-5 star items are significantly better. Look for higher quality items.

  • Check the star count on dropped items
  • 4-5 star items are worth keeping
  • Low quality items can be recycled

📚 Easy Magic

Easy Magic

Improves the enchanting system. You can combine enchantments more easily, remove specific enchantments, and have more control over what you want.

  • Modify enchantments without destroying the item
  • More control over enchantments vs the classic table
  • Combines well with the Disenchanting Table

🎰 Lucky Block

Lucky Block

Special blocks that, when broken, execute a random event. Can give you loot, kill you, spawn a boss, or a ton of other things. Fun but risky.

  • Never break them without being prepared
  • Build a wall behind you before mining them
  • Lucky Blocks are found in structures
  • The result is 100% random — sometimes great, sometimes fatal

⚙️ Multi-Piston

Multi-Piston

Pistons that can push multiple blocks at once. Perfect for giant doors, elevators and complex mechanisms.

  • Push up to 24 blocks
  • Variants: simple, sticky, advanced
  • Perfect with Create for automation

⛏️ FTB Ultimine

FTB Ultimine

Vein mining: mining one ore block mines all connected blocks of the same type. Hold the (~) key to enable the mode. HUGE time saver.

  • ~ key to activate
  • Mines entire ore veins at once
  • Works with trees
  • Configurable (durability consumed)

🏰 Valhelsia Structures

Valhelsia Structures

Large varied structures: forges, towers, ruins, abandoned castles. Each with its own loot and dangers. Very well integrated into the world.

  • More than 15 structure types
  • Progressive loot based on difficulty
  • Can contain spawners

⚔️ Equipment & Combat Avancé

🗡️ Soulslike Weaponry

Soulslike Weaponry

80+ weapons inspired by Dark Souls, Elden Ring and Bloodborne. Each weapon has a Weapon Art (special skill). Greatswords, scythes, halberds, whips, magic scepters.

  • Each weapon has a unique Weapon Art activated with Sneak+Attack
  • Claymore : Perseverance (stagger + boost armor)
  • Moonlight GS: Moonlight Barrage (lunar beams)
  • Dragon Slayer GS: Dragon Roar (massive AoE)
  • Craft with special materials depending on weapon

🏹 More Bows and Arrows

More Bows and Arrows

20+ new bows and arrow types. Ice bow, fire bow, explosive, multi-projectile arrows. Revolutionizes ranged combat.

  • Crossbow Repeater: automatic rapid fire
  • Longbow: double range, +50% damage
  • Frost Arrows: slows and freezes enemies
  • Explosive Arrows: 5-block radius AoE
  • Arrows craftable with special materials

🔱 Better Tridents

Better Tridents

Craftable and upgradeable tridents. No need to farm Drowned! New special enchantments for tridents, elemental variants.

  • Craft: 3 Prismarine Shards + elemental material
  • Fire Trident: fire damage + flame on impact
  • Thunder Trident: lightning on impact (no need for rain)
  • Trident Launcher: ×3 range with improved Riptide

🛡️ Shield Experience

Shield Experience

Generates XP each time your shield blocks an attack. The more damage blocked, the more XP earned. Rewards active defensive play.

  • Blocking in combat = passive XP source
  • Compatible with all modpack shields
  • Combines with Responsive Shields
  • Shield Experience enchantment available on shields

🔨 Just Hammers

Just Hammers

Multi-block hammers. Mine/break 3×3 blocks in one hit. Essential for quickly clearing large areas or mining efficiently.

  • 3×3 Hammer: mines a grid of 9 blocks simultaneously
  • Available in all materials (wood → netherite)
  • Durability decreases 9× faster (normal)
  • Combined with FTB Ultimine = ultra-fast mining

💫 Rings of Ascension

Rings of Ascension

Magic rings equipped in Curios slots. Each ring gives a unique movement ability: flight, double-jump, speed, absorption.

  • Ring of Ascension: free flight (like Elytra but hands-free)
  • Ring of the Enderchest: Ender Chest access anywhere
  • Ring of Regeneration: constant passive regeneration
  • Farmable in dungeons or craftable with rare items

⚗️ Easy Magic

Easy Magic

Simplified enchantments. Re-enchant an item without losing existing enchantments. Remove enchantments individually. End of frustrating RNG.

  • Reroll enchantments on the enchanting table
  • Remove an enchantment without losing everything
  • Cost in Lapis + XP based on enchantment level
  • Compatible with all enchantable items

📖 Enchantment Descriptions

Enchantment Descriptions

Detailed descriptions of each enchantment on hover in inventory. No more mystery enchantments — know exactly what each level does.

  • Hover over an enchanted item = full description
  • Shows exact values (+20% damage, etc.)
  • Covers vanilla and mod enchantments
  • Essential for understanding Soulslike enchantments

🧪 Disenchanting Table

Disenchanting Table

Special table to extract enchantments from an item onto a book. Recover enchantments from a worn item to transfer onto a new one.

  • Craft: Obsidian + Bookshelf + Diamonds
  • Recovers 1 random enchantment per use
  • The source item loses the extracted enchantment
  • Excellent for recycling looted equipment with good enchants

🪖 Armor of the Ages

Armor of the Ages

Historical armors from different eras: bronze, improved chainmail, medieval plate, Japanese, Roman. Each with unique stats and bonuses.

  • Samurai Armor: speed +10%, katana bonus
  • Legionnaire Armor: +fire and poison resistance
  • Knight Plate: best physical protection mid-game
  • Craft with era-specific materials (copper, iron, steel)

💎 Cataclysm Artifacts

Cataclysm Artifacts

Special items exclusive drops from Cataclysm bosses. Amulets, orbs, power fragments. Equipped in Curios slots for massive endgame bonuses.

  • Drops: Eyeless Lord, The Cataclysm, Mother of Mowzies
  • Each artifact = unique bonus (brief invincibility, AoE, heal)
  • Non-craftable, boss drops only
  • The best endgame gear alongside Cataclysm Weaponry

🏗️ Building & Decoration

🍄 Chipped + Rechiseled

Chipped / Rechiseled / Chisel & Chipped

Hundreds of variants for each block in the game. One stone brick can have 50+ texture variations. Essential for avoiding repetitive builds.

  • Chipped Workbench: open to see all available variants
  • Same craft as the original block, just different appearance
  • Compatible with Rechiseled for even more variants
  • Perfect for masonry, paving, tiles, worked wood

🪑 Another Furniture

Another Furniture

50+ decorative furniture: chairs, tables, shelves, sofas, lamps, counters. Wood style matching by biome. Makes interiors truly alive.

  • Chair: place + sit (right-click)
  • Table: combine multiple for a large table
  • Shelf: decorative storage (works like a chest)
  • Simple craft with planks + wool/iron depending on furniture

🛋️ Refurbished Furniture

Refurbished Furniture

Furniture with more materials and styles. Sofas, decorative beds, desks, wardrobes. Victorian to modern style depending on material used.

  • Wardrobe: 54-slot storage hidden in furniture
  • Desk: integrated crafting table with decoration
  • Compatible with Another Furniture for complete interiors

🏛️ Valhelsia Furniture

Valhelsia Furniture

Valhelsia-style furniture (elegant, medieval). Coffee tables, candelabras, tapestries, decorative bookshelves. Perfect for castles and manors.

  • Candelabra: decorative lighting without Redstone
  • Tapestry: customizable with banners
  • Decorative bookshelf: does not store books but very beautiful

🪟 Macaw's Windows, Doors & Bridges

Macaw's (MCW)

Complete collection of windows, doors, trapdoors, fences, bridges and paths. Dozens of styles per category for detailed architecture.

  • Windows: stained glass, slate, modern, medieval
  • Bridges: wood, stone, metal, suspension
  • Doors: saloon, barn, arched, gate
  • Paths: gravel, concrete, cobblestone, dirt

🛋️ Craft Furniture Mod (CFM)

Craft Furniture Mod

Functional furniture: stove, dishwasher, fridge (cold storage), bathtub, shower. Truly livable house with modern appliances.

  • Fridge: stores food, keeps it fresh
  • Stove: faster cooking than vanilla furnace
  • Sink: water access without moving
  • Sofa: sit, recover stamina

🪴 Twigs

Twigs

Natural decorative blocks: twigs, rocks, bulbs, botanical frames, lanterns. Enriches biomes and interiors with organic textures.

  • Pebbles: scatter on the ground to naturalize
  • Bundled Twigs: decorative wood pile
  • Colored Lanterns: tinted lighting
  • Frames: decorated frames with plants

🏗️ Prefab

Prefab

Instantly buildable prefab structures. Starter house, barn, mine, forge, tower. Ideal for starting quickly without building.

  • Structure Wand: choose and place a structure
  • Cost: matériaux listés avant construction
  • Starter House: wood + stone, ready in 30 seconds
  • Mine: automatic staircase down to Y=-60

🎋 Bamboo Everything

Bamboo Everything

Bamboo used for everything: planks, tools, armor, decorative blocks. Complete bamboo material set lighter than wood.

  • Bamboo tools: tier between wood and stone
  • Bamboo planks: unique building blocks
  • Bamboo armor: light, good resistance
  • Source: bamboo jungle, fast to farm

🌿 Bonsai Trees

Bonsai Trees

Miniature potted trees that grow automatically and passively drop their resources. Wood, apple, leaf farm with no effort.

  • Craft: pot + dirt + sapling
  • Auto-harvest every few minutes
  • Each tree = wood + species-specific resources
  • Ideal for passive indoor farming

🪨 Stoneworks

Stoneworks

Additional worked stone blocks. All stone types (granite, diorite, andesite, etc.) in cut, carved, polished, raw versions. Extended building palette.

  • Each vanilla stone = 6 worked variants
  • Craft with Stonecutter only
  • Mix polished granite + cut diorite = impressive walls

🏛️ Corail Pillar

Corail Pillar

Decorative pillars in all materials. Ionic, Doric, Corinthian. Essential for temples, castles, and columned buildings.

  • Sizes: half-pillar, full pillar, capital
  • All materials: wood, stone, marble, obsidian
  • Combine with Chipped for textured variants

🌅 Dawn of Time Builder

Dawn of Time Builder

Additional architectural blocks: arches, vaults, friezes, cornices. Enables constructions with curves and details impossible in vanilla.

  • Arches: perfect curves without workarounds
  • Gothic vaults: for cathedrals and dungeons
  • Decorative friezes: detailed wall borders

🔧 Utilitaires & Interface

🗺️ JourneyMap

JourneyMap

Minimap and full world map. Automatic mapping while exploring. Waypoints, markers, map sharing in multiplayer. The most complete minimap in the modpack.

  • J: open full-screen map
  • Waypoints: right-click on map to create a marker
  • Sharing: send waypoints to other players
  • Topography: 3D relief view available
  • Configurable minimap (size, zoom, position)

🔍 Jade (HWYLA)

Jade

Displays info on the block or mob you look at: name, source mod, remaining HP, machine content. Jade Colonies adds MineColonies info.

  • Hover block: name + source mod
  • Mob: current/max HP + active statuses
  • Machine (Create, Minecolonies): status + inventory
  • Configure display in Options → Jade

📦 JEI + JER

Just Enough Items / Just Enough Resources

JEI: all crafting recipes in the modpack. JER: drop rates for each mob, ore layers. Essential for knowing how to craft anything.

  • R on an item: shows all recipes to obtain it
  • U on an item: shows all crafts using that item
  • JER: ore layers, mob drop %
  • Search bar at the bottom to find any item

🎯 Neat

Neat

Floating health bars above all mobs. Displays name, current HP, max HP, active status icons. Know at a glance if a boss is almost dead.

  • Red bar = hostile enemy
  • Green bar = passive mob
  • Status icons: poison, fire, slow, etc.
  • Configure display size and distance

🧭 Structure Compass + Explorer's Compass

Structure Compass / Explorer's Compass

Two compasses to locate structures and biomes. Structure Compass points to the chosen structure. Explorer's Compass points to the chosen biome.

  • Right-click: open selection menu
  • Structure: Stronghold, Dungeon, Mansion, etc.
  • Biome: Mushroom Island, Bamboo, Cherry Grove, etc.
  • Essential for finding End portals, boss locations

⭐ Advancement Plaques + Better Advancements

Advancement Plaques / Better Advancements

Advancements displayed as a beautiful golden plaque on screen. Better Advancements reorganizes the advancements interface to be more readable and filterable.

  • Plaque: elegant animation on each advancement
  • Better Advancements: filter by mod, category
  • View progress: how many advancements remaining
  • ⚠️ Some advancements guide progression — follow them

📬 Pickup Notifier

Pickup Notifier

Displays in a screen corner each item picked up with quantity. Instantly know what you just looted without opening inventory.

  • Notification bottom right by default
  • Groups similar items together
  • Configurable display duration
  • Essential for knowing what bosses drop

🎒 Inventory Profiles Next

Inventory Profiles Next

Automatic inventory sorting in one click. Sort buttons in all inventories and chests. Organize by type, alphabetically, or custom.

  • Sort button appears automatically in chests
  • R: sort main inventory
  • Config: custom sorting rules
  • Lock slots: lock certain slots for important items

🔎 Searchables

Searchables

Search bar in enchantment lists, potions, and other menus with many options. Find the right enchantment by typing its name.

  • Works in: enchanting table, JEI, Creative
  • Type 3+ letters to filter instantly
  • Compatible with mod enchantments

📦 FTB Chunks + FTB Quests

FTB Chunks / FTB Quests

FTB Chunks: chunk claiming and protection. FTB Quests: quest system with rewards to guide progression. Two essential server tools.

  • Chunks: Claim = nobody can grief your blocks
  • Force Load: chunks loaded even without a player present (auto farms)
  • Quests: progression guide with item rewards
  • FTB Quests: access via dedicated key (see controls)

🔮 Ore Excavation / Veinminer

Ore Excavation / Veinst

Configurable vein mining. Mine an entire connected ore vein at once. Configure keys and limits to preference.

  • Hold configured key + mine = vein mine
  • Default limit: 64 blocks per vein mine
  • Consumes proportional durability
  • Compatible with Fortune and Silk Touch

🌟 Extra Quests

Extra Quests

Additional quests to guide the exploration of each dimension and mod. Objectives with special rewards to encourage full exploration.

  • Quests by dimension: Aether, Twilight, End, Nether
  • Rewards: unique non-craftable items
  • Progress tracker visible in the menu
  • Ideal for knowing what to do next

🌿 Ambiance, Nature & Divers

🌳 Dynamic Trees

Dynamic Trees

Trees that grow naturally and realistically. Trunks that widen with age, dynamic branches, cascade fall when chopped. No more floating trees to cut.

  • Cut the base = the entire tree falls automatically
  • Trees grow progressively from sapling
  • Compatible with Aether and Twilight Forest (dedicated Dynamic Trees mods)

🌅 Stellar View

Stellar View

Magnified night sky. Realistic stars by constellations, visible planets, detailed Milky Way, northern lights in cold biomes.

  • Northern lights: taiga and tundra on clear nights
  • Detailed moon with visible craters
  • Planets: bright moving points in the sky
  • Enable Shaders for maximum effect

🎵 Biome Music + Prominent OST

Biome Music / Prominent OST

Ambient music specific to each biome and dimension. Epic OST for boss fights. Sound immersion completes the visual.

  • Each biome has its own music track
  • Boss fight: automatic epic music
  • Dimensions: unique themes for Aether, TF, etc.

🍂 Falling Leaves

Falling Leaves

Leaf particles falling from trees in autumn (Serene Seasons). Cherry trees that snow pink petals. Magnificent visual effect.

  • Sakura: continuous pink petals
  • Serene Seasons autumn: orange/red leaves
  • Minimal FPS impact (well optimized)
  • Configure particle density if needed

🌌 Auroras

Auroras

Northern lights in cold biomes. Colorful light effects in the night sky, adapted by season. Complements Stellar View.

  • Visible on clear nights in taiga, tundra, arctic biomes
  • Variable colors: green, purple, blue
  • More intense in Serene Seasons winter

🏷️ Villager Names

Villager Names

Each villager now has a random first name displayed above their head. Recognize your favorite traders. Compatible with MineColonies for colonists.

  • Random names based on biome/village culture
  • MineColonies sync: colonists also have names
  • Persistent names: even after server restart

🎭 Japanese Culture

Japanese Culture

Japanese-inspired blocks and structures. Torii, shoji lanterns, tatami, decorative katana. Perfect for building a Japanese village or temple.

  • Torii Gate: decorative Shinto gate
  • Tatami: Japanese floor with regeneration bonus
  • Decorative katana: on walls, not usable as a weapon
  • Generates Japanese villages in bamboo forest biomes

🪟 Diagonal Fences, Walls & Windows

Diagonal Fences / Walls / Windows

Fences, walls and windows placeable diagonally. Build angles, triangles, perfect sloped roofs. Revolutionizes roofs and windows.

  • Place diagonally: Shift + place on a corner
  • Compatible with all materials
  • Ideal for 45° roofs, octagonal towers
  • Connected diagonal windows

🚪 Sliding Doors

Sliding Doors

Sliding doors in all materials. Open horizontally like shoji doors, automatic or manual. Modern or Japanese style.

  • Placement: 2 blocks side by side = sliding door
  • Redstone: sliding door automation
  • Glass variant: see through when closed

🎪 Essential (Social)

Essential

Multiplayer social features. Play with friends without a server, cosmetics, poses, emotes. Allows inviting friends directly into solo worlds.

  • Invite friends: solo world becomes multiplayer instantly
  • Cosmetics: capes, hats, accessories (optional)
  • Emotes: in-game character animations
  • ⚠️ Requires Essential account (free)

⚔️ Combat & Equipment

⚔️ Soulslike Weaponry

Soulslike Weaponry

80+ weapons inspired by Dark Souls, Elden Ring and Bloodborne. Each weapon has a special activatable art (L-click + Shift). Greatswords, scythes, halberds, spears, katanas.

  • Weapon Art: Shift + Right-click to activate (costs FP)
  • FP regenerates with rest or potions
  • Find in dungeon chests or craft with rare materials
  • Some weapons only drop from specific bosses
  • Scale with Strength or Dexterity (Puffish Attributes)

🏹 More Bows & Arrows

More Bows and Arrows

Arsenal of varied bows and arrows. Bows with special effects: Flame Bow, Frost Bow, Lightning Bow. Explosive, piercing, poisoned arrows.

  • Flame Bow: arrows that set targets on fire
  • Frost Bow: slows hit enemies
  • Explosive Arrows: small explosion radius
  • Craft with dimension materials: ice shards, blaze rods, etc.

🔨 Just Hammers

Just Hammers

3×3 zone mining hammers. As powerful as normal pickaxes but mine 9 blocks at once. Available in all materials.

  • Mine 3×3 = 9 blocks in one click
  • Perfect for quickly clearing caves
  • Fortune and Silk Touch work on all 9 blocks
  • Same craft as a pickaxe but in T shape

🐾 Mobs & Animaux

🐾 Critters & Companions

Critters and Companions

Adorable small companions to tame: Fennec Fox, Sea Bunny, Red Panda, Otter, Koi Fish, Dumbo Octopus. All unique and interactive.

  • Red Panda: tame with bamboo, follows the player
  • Otter: tame with fish, picks up items in water
  • Sea Bunny: found in oceans, very rare
  • Koi Fish: decorative, lives in ponds
  • Dumbo Octopus: deep ocean floor only

🐄 Apple Cows

Apple Cows

Special cows that drop apples instead of (or in addition to) meat. Several varieties by biome. Passive source of Golden Apples if fed correctly.

  • Drop: apples, golden apples (rare), enchanted apples (very rare)
  • Milk with bucket = Apple Juice (regeneration buff)
  • Breed on a farm = passive food source
  • Different varieties: Red Apple Cow, Green Apple Cow, Golden Apple Cow

⚔️ Illager Invasion

Illager Invasion

Much more intense and varied Pillager raids. New units: Illager Mage, Illager Brute, improved Illager Captain. Progressively harder raids.

  • Raids triggered by entering a village with Bad Omen
  • Illager Mage: casts spells (slowness, weakness, poison)
  • Illager Brute: very strong, knockback resistant
  • Improved raid rewards: better Hero of the Village loot

👮 Guard Villagers

Guard Villagers

Villagers that can be turned into armed guards to defend villages. Equippable with armor and weapons. Patrol automatically around the village.

  • Transform: give a sword to a villager
  • Equip with armor to increase their resistance
  • Archer guards: give a bow for ranged units
  • Very useful for protecting an outpost

🏗️ Building & Decoration

🌳 Bonsai Trees

Bonsai Trees 3

Miniature potted trees that automatically generate wood and resources. Place a sapling in a pot = passive wood farm in your base.

  • Craft: Bonsai Pot + any sapling
  • Generates wood, apples, leaves, sap based on tree type
  • Stack multiple pots for mass production
  • Improve with Fortune for better yield
  • Perfect for interior bases without forest access

🏠 Prefab

Prefab

Instant construction of prefab structures. Houses, farms, towers, mines, fortresses — place an entire structure in one click.

  • Open the Prefab interface with the construction book
  • 50+ available structures including houses, dungeons, farms
  • Structures in different styles (wood, stone, brick)
  • Ideal for building a base quickly early in the game
  • Structures often include basic furniture

🪵 Dynamic Trees

Dynamic Trees

Trees that grow dynamically and realistically. Trees start small and grow over time. Cut a tree = it naturally regrows.

  • Trees grow progressively (real minutes/hours)
  • Cut at the base = the entire tree falls automatically
  • No need to replant if left in its natural biome
  • Compatible with FTB Ultimine for fast cutting

🪨 Corail Pillar

Corail Pillar

New architectural pillar and column blocks. Dozens of types: marble, granite, quartz, obsidian. Perfect for epic builds.

  • Craft: base blocks + Pillar Block in shapeless
  • Compatible with Chipped and Rechiseled for more variants
  • Antique, medieval, modern styles available
  • Ideal for Greek/Roman column bases

🗺️ Exploration & Navigation

🧭 Structure Compass

Structure Compass

Compass that points to any structure generated in the world. Configure which structure to search, the compass shows the direction.

  • Simple craft with a compass + paper
  • Right-click to select the target structure
  • Points to: Stronghold, Village, Mansion, mod structures
  • Essential for finding the Stronghold (Eye of Ender alternative)
  • Works for all installed mod structures

🔭 Explorers Compass

Explorers Compass

Compass to locate specific biomes. Configure the desired biome, points in the right direction. Complementary to Structure Compass.

  • Search specific biomes: volcanoes (Fire Dragon), snowy mountains (Ice Dragon)
  • Find mod biomes (Terralith, Oh The Biomes)
  • Perfect for targeting rare biome resources

🌍 Scaling Health

Scaling Health

Mobs scale in difficulty with player progression. The more you progress, the stronger mobs become. Prevents the game from becoming too easy in endgame.

  • Mobs gagnent HP et dégâts selon ta progression
  • Enchantments and armor remain necessary even in endgame
  • Boss scaling: even harder if overleveled
  • Configurable: adjust the multiplier in settings

Complete treasure hunt. Buried treasure chests, treasure maps, hidden clues in the environment. Unique and precious loot.

  • Find treasure maps in structure chests
  • Maps indicate the location of a buried chest
  • Chests contain special weapons, rare materials, keys
  • Keys open locked chests in dungeons
  • Version Twilight Forest avec loot thématique

⚡ Quality of Life

🏺 Iron Chests & Iron Furnaces

Iron Chests / Iron Furnaces

Coffres et fourneaux améliorés en différents matériaux. Plus d'espace de stockage, fonte plus rapide selon le matériau.

  • Iron Chest : 54 slots (double vanille)
  • Gold Chest : 81 slots
  • Diamond Chest : 108 slots
  • Crystal Chest : contenu visible de l'extérieur
  • Iron Furnace : fonte 2× plus rapide, Gold Furnace 4×

🪄 Easy Magic & Disenchanting

Easy Magic / Disenchanting Table

Improved enchantment control. Easy Magic allows re-rolling enchantments at the table. Disenchanting Table extracts enchantments onto books.

  • Easy Magic: retry enchantments without moving the item
  • Disenchanting Table: extract enchantment → book (XP cost)
  • Saves enormous amounts of XP and lapis
  • Indispensable pour optimiser l'équipement endgame

🧲 Inventory Totem

Inventory Totem

Totem of Undying that works from inventory (no need to hold it in hand). The totem in any inventory slot saves you.

  • Place in any inventory slot
  • S'active automatiquement si mort imminente
  • Libère les deux mains pour combattre
  • Combiné avec Void Totem = double protection

📊 Enhanced Boss Bars

Enhanced Boss Bars

Barres de vie des boss améliorées. Affichage HP exact, phases du boss, icône du boss, effets visuels sur la barre selon l'état du boss.

  • HP exact affiché (ex: "2450 / 5000")
  • Barre change de couleur aux phases importantes
  • Icône du boss visible sur la barre
  • Indicateur de rage/buff du boss

🎵 Biome Music & Prominent OST

Biome Music / Prominent OST

Musiques ambiantes par biome et OST principal du modpack. Chaque biome a sa propre musique thématique. L'OST change selon la situation (combat, exploration, boss).

  • Musiques uniques pour chaque dimension
  • Combat : musique intense automatique quand mob hostile proche
  • Boss : thème épique dédié pour chaque boss majeur
  • Régler volume dans Options → Music

⚖️ Ore Excavation & Veinst

Ore Excavation / Veinst

Two vein mining mods complementary to FTB Ultimine. Veinst = automatic vein mining on ores. Ore Excavation = configurable area excavation.

  • Veinst: Shift + mine triggers automatic vein mine
  • Ore Excavation: configure excavation shape (line, area, cube)
  • Ne pas utiliser les trois en même temps — choisir un seul
  • FTB Ultimine recommandé comme principal

🎮 Gameplay & Survival — Essential Mods

🌊 Aquaculture 2

Aquaculture 2

Extended fishing system: 30+ fish species, upgradeable rods, bait, fishing boxes with loot. Fishing becomes a real profession.

  • 30+ fish depending on biome and depth
  • Craftable rods with bonuses (Luck, durability)
  • Tackle Box: store bait and accessories
  • Rare fish = special crafts (Neptune armor)
  • Use Alex's Mobs larvae as bait

⚖️ Scaling Health

Scaling Health

Mobs gain HP based on distance from spawn and number of players. World progressively harder the further you go. Ideal for balancing the modpack in groups.

  • Mobs far from spawn = HP × 2 to × 10
  • Adaptive scaling based on number of players
  • Neat health bars display scaled HP
  • Prepare solid equipment before distant exploration

🎒 Useful Backpacks

Useful Backpacks

Backpacks with multiple inventory sizes. Equippable in the back slot (Curios). Progressive bag upgrades based on invested resources.

  • Sizes: Small (9 slots) → Medium (18) → Large (27) → Huge (54)
  • Craft: Leather + String depending on desired size
  • Opens with dedicated key without opening inventory
  • Upgrade in place without transferring contents

📦 More Chest Variants

More Chest Variants

Chests in all wood materials (acacia, dark oak, mangrove, bamboo, cherry). Perfect for organizing by construction theme.

  • Same capacity as vanilla chest
  • Perfect for visual consistency of bases
  • Bamboo chest: light and quick to craft

🎯 Tectonic

Tectonic

Massively improved Overworld terrain generation. Higher mountains, deep valleys, plateaus, canyons. Complements Terralith for epic terrain.

  • Mountains up to Y=320
  • Deep canyons down to Y=-60
  • Works in synergy with Terralith
  • New world generation recommended to benefit

🧭 Explorify

Explorify

Base vanilla structure improvements: reworked caves, enriched nether wastes, plains with natural details. Fills vanilla's visual gaps.

  • Caves: stalactites, vegetation, natural details
  • Nether Wastes: accentuated relief, lava pools
  • Plains: scattered rocks, plant variety

🎵 Traveler's Titles

Traveler's Titles

Title displayed on screen when entering a new biome or dimension. "You have entered: Terralith's Highlands" in beautiful cinematic text.

  • Display at first step in an unknown biome
  • RPG style: title on semi-transparent dark background
  • Covers all biomes from all mods
  • Configure duration and style in Options

🔑 Inventory Totem

Inventory Totem

Resurrection totem usable from inventory (no need in hand). Place the totem in your inventory and it activates automatically at death.

  • Place in any inventory slot
  • Automatic activation at death — hands free
  • Combined with Void Totem = maximum survival
  • ⚠️ Consumed on each use

🌀 Multi Piston

Multi Piston

Pistons that can push up to 64 blocks instead of 12. Revolutionizes Redstone mechanisms and Create contraptions that use pistons.

  • Power piston: configurable from 1 to 64 blocks
  • Ideal for Redstone elevators on great heights
  • Compatible with Create for complex contraptions
  • Craft: Piston + Blaze Rod

🔭 Oculus (Shaders)

Oculus

Shader support for Forge. Compatible with Complementary, BSL, Sildur's and other major shaderpacks. Visually transforms the modpack.

  • F3+A: reload shaders after change
  • Complementary Reimagined: best quality/fps balance
  • BSL Shaders: magnificent cloud and water effects
  • Disable if FPS too low (K key by default)
  • Compatible with Euphoria Patcher (included in pack)

🪟 Double Doors

Double Doors

Double doors open simultaneously with a single click. Portals and large entrances open in one elegant movement.

  • Place 2 doors side by side = synchronized auto activation
  • Compatible with all doors (vanilla + mods)
  • Also works with double trapdoors

🍖 Eating Animation

Eating Animation

3D hand animation when eating an item. See the bread, apple or potion approach the mouth. Small immersion detail that changes everything.

  • Visible in first and third person
  • Covers vanilla + mod food
  • Unique animation per item type (drinking vs eating)

🛠️ Visual Workbench

Visual Workbench

Items placed on the Crafting Table remain visible on the table in 3D. See in real time what is being crafted on all crafting tables.

  • 3D items placed on the table during crafting
  • Compatible with mod crafting tables
  • No performance impact

💀 The Cataclysm Universe — Complete Endgame Content

Cataclysm Weaponry 2.0

Arsenal of legendary weapons crafted with Cataclysm boss materials. The most powerful weapons in the modpack. Each has active special effects.

  • Requires boss drop materials: Eyeless, Ancient Remnant, etc.

  • Runic Blade: active runes, magic damage
  • Each weapon = 1 boss minimum to defeat for materials

Cataclysm Tools

Post-Cataclysm crafted tools. Pickaxe, axe, shovel more efficient than Netherite. Materials harvested from bosses, near-infinite durability.

Mowzies Cataclysm

Cross-content between Mowzie's Mobs and L'Ender's Cataclysm. New interactions, cross bosses, hybrid loot, drops combining both mods.

  • Cataclysm recipes that require Mowzies drops

🏺 Aslan's Cataclysm + Azverix's

Aslan's Cataclysm / Azverix's Cataclysm

Cataclysm mod extensions. New bosses, structures, additional weapons and armor that extend endgame beyond base content.

🧰 Cataclysm UT Lite

Cataclysm UT Lite

Utilities and tweaks for L'Ender's Cataclysm. Balancing, new alternative recipes, quality of life for Cataclysm endgame.

⚡ Xenos Cataclysm

Xenos Cataclysm

New Cataclysm branch oriented toward magic and spells. Elemental bosses, grimoires, activatable spells. The magical endgame of the modpack.

EC LEC Plugin

Compatibility plugin between L'Ender's Cataclysm and other mods. Adds cross recipes and interactions between different systems.

Default Skill Trees

Default skill trees for the Puffish Skills system. Defines available branches and their skill point cost.

  • Branches: Combat, Magic, Exploration, Crafting
  • Some skills require Cataclysm items to unlock

🔩 Misc — Storage, Visuals & QoL

📊 Overflowing Bars

Overflowing Bars

Health and hunger bars that overflow visually when they exceed the vanilla maximum. Compatibility with HP increased by Scaling Health and bosses.

  • HP above 20 displayed in extra bars
  • Color changes according to health level
  • Compatible with Armor of the Ages, Artifacts HP

🌿 Leaves Be Gone

Leaves Be Gone

Leaves disappear instantly when a trunk is cut instead of decaying slowly. Fell a tree = everything goes at the same time.

  • Compatible with Dynamic Trees (trees fall together)
  • Configurable: disappearance speed
  • Collect Saplings and Apples before they disappear

🏗️ Domum Ornamentum

Domum Ornamentum

Hybrid blocks that combine two different materials. Create a wood plank textured with stone, or unique custom blocks. Infinite combinations.

  • Hybrid block: 1 base block + 1 overlay block = new block
  • Used by MineColonies for buildings
  • Available in all building materials
  • Craft with the dedicated Domum Crafting Table

Towering Townscape

Vertical buildings and towers generated in villages. Denser villages, multi-floor architecture, guard towers, stacked houses.

  • Compatibility with Towns & Towers
  • More villagers = more available trades

Town Talk

Villagers talk! Dialogue bubbles above the head with contextual phrases depending on their job, time of day, and events.

  • Blacksmith: "I need iron!" when his chest is empty
  • Villager at night: "I hear zombies..."
  • Raid in progress: cries of panic
  • Makes villages lively and expressive

Celestisynth / Medieval Music

All wood types from modern biomes added for furniture mods. Cherry, Mangrove, Bamboo wood compatibility with CFM, Another Furniture, etc.

Structory / Structory Towers

Atmospheric structures scattered throughout the Overworld. Structory: small points of interest. Towers: isolated towers with guardians and loot.

  • Towers: towers with mini boss at the top
  • Loot proportional to tower difficulty

⚔️ Valhelsia Structures

Valhelsia Structures

Valhelsia-style structures in Overworld and Nether. Elegant medieval architecture, carefully crafted dungeons, cut stone forts.

  • Distinctive style: black stone + dark wood
  • Superior quality loot
  • Loot Integrations compatibility

🌸 Pale Garden

Pale Garden

Biome Overworld rare à l'atmosphère apaisante mais trompeuse — fleurs pâles à perte de vue, brume légère, lumière diffuse. Introduit le Pale Oak, a unique decorative ivory wood, as well as Creaking, silent tree mobs that only move when you're not looking at them.

  • Locate with Explorer's Compass → "Pale Garden"
  • Pale Oak Logs: off-white wood ideal for bright interior decoration
  • Creaking: enemy only moves OUT of your field of vision — turn around often
  • Rare loot: Resin Clumps → Resin Bricks (new amber building material)
  • No hostility during the day — dangerous at night with Creaking active en masse
  • Ideal for building a calm and luminous themed base

🌊 Call from the Depth

Call from the Depth

Aquatic extension that adds deep-sea marine creatures and enriches underwater exploration. Unfathomable abysses under the oceans hide Lovecraftian horrors.

  • Creatures: Deep Horror (giant octopus), Abyssal Lurker (abyss shark), Void Jellyfish
  • Deep Horror: 80 hearts, blinding ink, paralysis — Water Breathing + Night Vision mandatory
  • Abyssal Trench: underwater trench generated below Y=-40 — new exploration zone
  • Abyss loot: Abyssal Scales (resistant aquatic armor), Deep Crystal (optics crafting)
  • Synergy with Atlantis — CftD creatures populate the outskirts of the sunken city
  • Diving beacon: place a Conduit before exploring the Trenches

♾️ Infinite Abyss

Infinite Abyss

Endgame dimension of infinite exploration — a bottomless pit plunged into the Void. Impossible architectures, gravity-defying physics, enemies only from the Void. The ultimate modpack challenge for explorers.

  • Access: portal craft with Deep Crystal × 4 + Void Core from Cataclysm bosses
  • Gravity is reversed in zones — use Elytra + Fireworks to navigate
  • Each tier offers progressively better loot — go as low as possible
  • Tier 10: Abyssal Armor set (Void resistance, best in game for this stat)
  • Tier 25: Infinite Fragment — needed for certain Stellar Conquest crafts
  • ALWAYS have a Void Totem — falling off platforms = infinite fall

💠 Cataclysm Artifacts

Cataclysm Artifacts

Legendary passive items dropped only by L'Ender's Cataclysm bosses. Each equips in a dedicated Curios slot and offers a permanent endgame-rank passive power.

  • Soul Render Fragment : equipped in Curios → +15% damage to all bosses
  • Ignitium Heart : regenerates 1 heart every 30s in combat — drop from The Furnace
  • Void Eye : see through walls within a 10-block radius — drop from The Remnant
  • Ender Shield Core : absorbs 30% of Cataclysm damage — Ender Guardian drop
  • Harbinger's Mark : +30% movement speed after a boss kill — The Harbinger drop
  • All are equippable simultaneously if you have 5 Curios slots available

Utility Mods & Quality of Life

Mods that improve the daily gameplay experience — navigation, interfaces, optimization, comfort. Essential for fully enjoying the modpack.

  • See players in real time (multiplayer)

  • Easy waypoint sharing

📦 Interface & Inventory

📖 JEI (Just Enough Items)

JEI

THE modpack bible. See all crafting recipes, search any item, understand how to get each resource. Press R on an item = see its recipe.

  • R key: see the crafting recipe
  • U key: see an item's uses
  • Search bar in the bottom right
  • Bookmark (A key) for favorites

📊 JER (Just Enough Resources)

JER

JEI extension that shows drop rates for each mob, ores by dimension, chest loot tables. Know EXACTLY where to find what you're looking for.

  • See each mob's drops with %
  • Ore distribution by layer
  • Structure loot tables

Upgradeable backpacks with modules (auto-sorting, crafting, filters). The ultimate backpack of the modpack — much better than Useful Backpacks.

  • Upgrades: increase size, add filters
  • Built-in crafting module
  • Automatic sorting by category
  • Lock important slots

Inventory Profiles Next

Automatically sort inventory in one click (R key by default). Quickly move entire stacks, automatically replace broken tools.

  • R key: auto-sort

  • Auto-refill: replaces broken tools

Searchables

Search through all nearby chests from your inventory. No need to open each chest one by one to find what you're looking for.

  • Works on all nearby chests

Jade

Displays mob health as a bar above their head + floating damage dealt. Essential for knowing if you are effective in combat.

Guard Villagers

Zombies become MUCH more dangerous: they smell blood, hear sounds, work in packs. The night becomes a real challenge.

Upon death, a corpse appears at your location with all your items. More immersive than Tombstone — you must go back to retrieve your corpse.
