⚡ Performance & Technical

⚡ Sodium / BadOptimizations

Sodium, BadOptimizations

Optimisation du rendu graphique. +50% FPS minimum sur la plupart des configurations. ESSENTIEL pour jouer confortablement avec 250+ mods.

  • Gains de FPS massifs
  • Pas de perte de qualité visuelle
  • Compatible avec shaders (Iris)

🔥 Spark

Spark

Profiler de performance pour identifier les lags. Permet de voir quels mods ou chunks causent des problèmes de performance.

  • Commande /spark pour profiler
  • Génère des rapports détaillés
  • Identify lag sources

🌊 Better Chunk Loading

Better Chunk Loading

Optimizes chunk loading — fewer freezes when exploring quickly. The game stays smooth even while flying with Elytra.

  • Progressive loading
  • Less stuttering
  • Essentiel pour l'exploration rapide

📉 Better FPS Distance

Better FPS Distance

Reduces details of distant entities to improve FPS. Mobs far from you are visually simplified.

  • FPS gains in mass combat
  • Configurable (simplification distance)
  • Imperceptible visuellement

🔊 Sound Physics Remastered

Sound Physics Remastered

Realistic sounds with reverb, echo, attenuation through walls. Audio becomes much more immersive — caves resonate, sounds are muffled behind doors.

  • Reverb in the grottes
  • Sounds muffled through walls
  • Extreme audio immersion
  • Minimal FPS impact

Torches in your hand illuminate around you. Very handy for exploring without constantly placing torches.

  • Torch in hand = mobile light
  • Works with all light-emitting items
  • Optional (minimal FPS cost)

💾 Smooth Chunk Save

Smooth Chunk Save

Progressive chunk saving to avoid freezes. The game stays smooth even during auto-saves.

  • No freeze on /save
  • Saves in the background
  • Essential in multiplayer

💧 Clumps

Clumps

XP orbs merge into large orbs instead of hundreds of small ones. Huge FPS gain in XP farms.

  • Automatically merges XP orbs
  • Massive FPS gains in XP farms
  • Faster collection

🗺️ Chunky — Chunk Pre-generation (Performance)

✅ Chunky — Already Included in the Modpack!

  • ✅ Chunky IS included: Chunky-1.3.146.jar is already in the /mods/ folder
  • Role: Pre-generate terrain BEFORE playing — eliminates exploration lag
  • Usage: Generate chunks around spawn before starting the game for a smooth world
  • ⚠️ Not to be confused: FTB Chunks = base claiming/protection · Chunky = terrain pre-generation/performance
  • Version: 1.3.146 (compatible Forge 1.20.1) + ChunkyChunks for bonus features

📥 How to Use Chunky

1️⃣ Launch the Game

  • Chunky already installed: No installation required
  • Verification: Type /chunky in chat — if it works, you're good!
  • Version included: Chunky 1.3.146 compatible with Forge 1.20.1

2️⃣ Installation

  • Locate mods folder: [instance_modpack]/mods/
  • Copy the .jar: Drag chunky-forge-X.X.X.jar into /mods/
  • Restart Minecraft: Relaunch the launcher
  • Verification: Type /chunky in chat — if command recognized = OK

🔧 Method 1: Automation via Datapack (RECOMMENDED)

📦 Auto-Start Datapack

This method uses a datapack that launches Chunky automatically on first world connection.

  • Advantages: Automatic, works solo and server, no external script
  • Downsides: Triggers after world creation (not during)
  • Ideal for: Solo players and small servers

Step 1: Create the Datapack

  • Create folder: [world]/datapacks/chunky_auto/
  • File pack.mcmeta: Datapack metadata
  • Function file: data/chunky_auto/functions/start.mcfunction
  • Full structure: See below

Step 2: Datapack Files

pack.mcmeta :
{
  "pack": {
    "pack_format": 15,
    "description": "Auto Chunky Pregen"
  }
}

data/chunky_auto/functions/start.mcfunction :
# Overworld
chunky radius 5000
chunky start
tellraw @a {"text":"[Chunky] Overworld pregen started (5000 radius)","color":"gold"}

📝 Datapack Activation

  • Create the world: New world with the desired seed
  • Exit immediately: Exit to menu
  • Copy the datapack: Into [saves]/[world_name]/datapacks/
  • Relaunch the world: Connect
  • Execute: /function chunky_auto:start
  • ⚠️ One-time use: Delete the datapack afterward to avoid re-triggering

🖥️ Method 2: Server Script (DEDICATED SERVERS)

🐧 Script Bash (Linux)

#!/bin/bash
# chunky_pregen.sh

echo "🗺️ Starting Chunky Pre-generation..."

# Start server in screen
screen -dmS minecraft java -Xmx12G -Xms12G -jar forge-server.jar nogui

# Wait for startup (60s)
echo "⏳ Waiting for server startup..."
sleep 60

# Overworld
echo "🌍 Pre-generating Overworld (5000 radius)..."
screen -S minecraft -p 0 -X stuff "chunky radius 5000^M"
sleep 2
screen -S minecraft -p 0 -X stuff "chunky start^M"

# Wait for Overworld completion (check logs)
echo "⏳ Waiting for Overworld completion..."
while ! grep -q "Task finished" logs/latest.log; do
  sleep 60
done

# Nether
echo "🔥 Pre-generating Nether (2500 radius)..."
screen -S minecraft -p 0 -X stuff "chunky world minecraft:the_nether^M"
sleep 2
screen -S minecraft -p 0 -X stuff "chunky radius 2500^M"
sleep 2
screen -S minecraft -p 0 -X stuff "chunky start^M"

# Wait for Nether completion
# ... (same pattern)

# Shutdown
echo "✅ Pre-generation complete. Stopping server..."
screen -S minecraft -p 0 -X stuff "stop^M"

echo "🎉 Done! Server ready for players."

Usage: chmod +x chunky_pregen.sh && ./chunky_pregen.sh

🪟 Script Batch (Windows)

@echo off
REM chunky_pregen.bat

echo Starting Chunky Pre-generation...

REM Start server
start "Minecraft" java -Xmx12G -Xms12G -jar forge-server.jar nogui

REM Wait for startup
timeout /t 60 /nobreak

REM Send commands (requires RCON or alternative)
REM Windows automation is complex — manual method recommended

echo Windows automation limited - use manual commands instead
pause

⚠️ Windows Limitation: No easy stdin piping — use manual method or RCON

⌨️ Méthode 3 : Commandes Manuelles (PLUS SIMPLE)

🎯 Complete Manual Procedure

  • 1. Create world: New world, optional seed
  • 2. Se connecter : Entrer dans le monde
  • 3. Overworld : /chunky radius 5000 → /chunky start
  • 4. Laisser tourner : 4-8 heures (overnight)
  • 5. Check progression : /chunky montre %
  • 6. Une fois fini : Passer au Nether

🔄 Séquence Complète Dimensions

Overworld :
/chunky radius 5000
/chunky start
# Attendre 4-8h

Nether :

/chunky radius 2500

The Aether :

/chunky start
# Attendre 1-3h

⏸️ Useful Controls

  • /chunky : View current progress (%)
  • /chunky pause : Pause
  • /chunky continue: Resume
  • /chunky cancel: Cancel completely
  • /chunky silent: Disable spam messages

⚙️ Configuration Avancée

📄 Fichier config/chunky.toml

After first Chunky launch, edit the config file:

[general]
# Vitesse génération (chunks/sec)
# Higher = faster but more lag
chunks-per-second = 20

# Buffer memory (MB)
memory-buffer = 2048

# Quiet mode (fewer messages)
quiet-mode = false

Recommendation: chunks-per-second = 10-15 for stable generation, 20-30 if powerful PC

💾 Optimisation RAM & CPU

  • RAM Allocation: Minimum 12GB for pre-gen (-Xmx12G -Xms12G)
  • Arguments JVM : -XX:+UseG1GC -XX:MaxGCPauseMillis=200
  • Render distance : Mettre à 2 pendant pré-gen (économie ressources)
  • Close applications: Chunky uses 100% available CPU
  • SSD recommended: Intense disk I/O — HDD = very slow

📊 Recommended Time & Radius

🌍 Overworld

  • Radius 3000: 6000×6000 blocks, 2-4h
  • Radius 5000: 10000×10000 blocks, 4-8h ⭐ RECOMMENDED
  • Radius 10000: 20000×20000 blocks, 16-30h (overkill)
  • Covers: Complete early + mid game

🔥 Nether

  • Radius 1250: Equivalent to 10000 Overworld, 1-2h
  • Radius 2500: Equivalent to 20000 Overworld, 2-4h ⭐
  • Note : Ratio 1:8 avec Overworld
  • Structures : Fortresses, Bastions garantis

🌑 The End

  • Radius 2000: Île principale + outer islands, 1-2h
  • Radius 3000 : Exploration extensive, 1-3h ⭐
  • Post-Dragon : Nullscape/Outer End actifs

🌙 Twilight Forest

  • Radius 2000 : Mid-game progression, 2-3h
  • Radius 3000 : Full progression 8 phases, 3-5h ⭐
  • Critique : Beaucoup de structures

☁️ The Aether

  • Radius 1500 : Dungeons Bronze/Silver, 1-2h
  • Radius 2000 : Full dungeons + Redux, 2-3h ⭐
  • Îles flottantes : Génération moins intensive

🌿 Autres Dimensions

  • Blue Skies : 1500-2000 radius, 1-2h
  • Undergarden : 1000 radius, 1h
  • Bumblezone : 1000 radius, 1h
  • Optionnel : Selon besoin exploration

🎯 OPTIMAL WORKFLOW — New World

  • Vendredi soir : Créer monde, lancer Overworld 5000 radius, laisser tourner la nuit
  • Samedi matin : Overworld fini (~8h), lancer Nether 2500 radius
  • Samedi midi : Nether fini (~4h), lancer End 3000 radius
  • Saturday afternoon: End done (~2h), launch Twilight Forest 3000 radius
  • Samedi soir : TF fini (~4h), lancer Aether 2000 radius
  • Dimanche matin : Aether fini (~2h) → TOTAL : ~20h
  • Dimanche : Jouer sans AUCUN lag de génération ! 🎉

⚠️ Common Issues

  • "Out of memory" : Augmenter RAM allocation (minimum 12GB)
  • Very slow generation: Normal with 250+ mods — be patient or reduce radius
  • Crash pendant pré-gen : RAM insuffisante, vérifier logs/latest.log
  • Chunks corrompus : Supprimer region files affectés, relancer pré-gen
  • Pause/Continue ne marche pas : Restart serveur/monde, /chunky continue
  • "Task already running" : /chunky cancel puis relancer

🎵 Atmosphere & Immersion

🎵 Biome Music

Biome Music

Each biome has its own ambient music. Deserts have oriental melodies, forests have soothing sounds, etc. Maximum audio immersion.

  • Unique music per biome
  • Configurable volume
  • Compatible with all mod biomes

Integrated in-game voice chat. Talk with your friends without Discord — voice is spatialized (louder if close, quieter if far).

  • Push-to-talk by default
  • Spatialized audio (3D)
  • Chat groups possible
  • Configurable (volume, distance)

🏔️ Traveler's Titles

Traveler's Titles

Displays the biome name in large on screen when entering a new biome. Very cinematic and immersive.

  • Styled title at biome entry
  • Configurable (duration, style)
  • Learn biome names

Villagers have unique names displayed above their head. More immersive than generic "Villager".

  • Unique procedural names
  • Compatible with Guard Villagers
  • Persistent names (saved)

🌸 Auroras

Auroras

Northern lights in cold biomes at night. Magnificent visual spectacle in snowy mountains and tundras.

  • Random appearance at night
  • Varied colors
  • No gameplay impact (purely visual)

🌺 Blossom

Blossom

Adds cherry blossom trees and other flowering trees. Magnificent flowering forest biomes in spring (Serene Seasons).

  • Japanese cherry trees
  • Seasonal flowers
  • Craftable cherry wood

🔧 Technical & Hidden Mods

📚 GeckoLib

GeckoLib

Animation library for mods. Required for Ice & Fire, Mowzie's Mobs, Alex's Mobs and many others. Does nothing alone.

  • Smooth animations for mobs
  • Required by many mods
  • Do not delete

🏛️ Citadel

Citadel

Library for Ice & Fire and other creature mods. Manages animations, AI and complex behaviors.

  • Required for Ice & Fire
  • Manages dragon AI
  • Do not delete

📐 Kotlin for Forge

Kotlin for Forge

Allows mods coded in Kotlin to function. Required by several mods in the pack.

  • Programming language
  • Required by certain mods
  • No visible effect in game

🔌 Connector / Forgified

Connector, Connector Extras

Allows Fabric mods to run on Forge. Considerably expands the available mod catalog.

  • Fabric→Forge compatibility
  • More mods available
  • Transparent to the player

🏗️ Structure Gel API

Structure Gel API

API for generating structures. Used by Yung's Mods and others. Improves world generation.

  • Optimized structure generation
  • Required for Yung's Mods

🎯 Recommended Mods to Enable

  • Sound Physics : The audio immersion is incredible — caves really echo.
  • Jade : Indispensable for seeing block/mob info — activate from the start.

Pro Tips

Advanced tips to master every aspect of the modpack. From navigation to optimization.

🗺️ Chunky — Quick Pre-generation

  • BEFORE playing: Pre-generate chunks with Chunky = zero exploration lag
  • Essential commands: /chunky radius 5000 then /chunky start
  • Overworld: 5000 radius (4-8h generation) — CRITICAL
  • Nether: 2500 radius (2-4h) — saves you from freezes
  • The End: 3000 radius (1-3h) — post-Dragon exploration
  • Mod dimensions: Twilight Forest, Aether (2000-3000 radius each)
  • ⚠️ Total: 20-40 hours — run overnight/weekend
  • 💡 Solo + good PC: A radius of 1500-2000 is more than enough for solo play on a powerful machine — the engine generates chunks on the fly without noticeable lag. The 5000 radius is mainly recommended for multiplayer servers or modest hardware configurations.
  • Why: 250+ mods make generation HEAVY — pre-gen avoids stuttering/freezes
  • Full guide: See section "Utility Mods → Performance → Chunky"

🗺️ Navigation & Exploration

  • JourneyMap: Automatic mapping. Mark points of interest (spawners, structures, dungeons). Share the map in multiplayer.
  • Structure Compass: Points to any structure in the game. Essential for finding Strongholds (Ender Dragon) and boss structures.
  • Explorer's Compass: Points to specific biomes. Looking for a volcanic biome? An icy biome? In seconds.
  • Waystones: Place outside boss zones to return quickly after a death. In multiplayer: all players can use the same Waystones.
  • Explorify: Adds rewards for exploring new biomes. Incentivizes travel — and you will find more structures.
  • Dragon Finder / Dragon Seeker: To locate Ice & Fire Dragons on the map — essential for finding them.

⚔️ Combat & Survival

  • Regen Potions: Craft in large quantities BEFORE boss fights. Regen III is your lifeline. Automated Brewing Stands (Create) give you them in bulk.
  • Expanded Combat: Adds advanced combat mechanics: parry, dodges, improved blocking with the shield. Master these mechanics = survive much better.
  • Soulslike Weaponry: Souls-like weapons with special moves. Very effective in combat. Craft them as soon as you can.
  • Passive Artifacts: Equip Artifacts that give regen, resistance or permanent health. Even outside combat, they help you survive.
  • Scaling Health — strategy: Kill mobs regularly to increase your max health. Build a farm = infinite health over time.
  • Shields: Shield Experience generates XP when blocking. In solo, a shield in the off-hand is ALWAYS recommended — blocking melee hits saves your life.
  • Combat Shrines: Look for Shrines for temporary combat bonuses. Perfect before a boss.

🏗️ Building & Automation

  • Create — Shafts & Cogwheels: Source of mechanical power. Connect to machines to automate production. A shaft + water wheel = free power.
  • Create — Conveyor Belt: Move items automatically between your farms and machines. The foundation of any automated system.
  • Create — Deployer: Places or retrieves blocks automatically. Perfect for automated farms (planting seeds, harvesting).
  • MineColonies: Create a colony with automated citizens. The Miner digs, the Farmer cultivates, the Builder builds. An entire automated base.
  • FTB Ultimine: Mine blocks in bulk by holding the key. Very handy for clearing areas quickly.
  • Chipped & Rechiseled: Customize your blocks with unique patterns. Make your base truly unique and beautiful.
  • Prefab: Pre-built houses you can place directly. For a quick shelter at the start of the game.

📦 Inventory Management

  • JEI (Just Enough Items): Your modpack bible. Search any item, see its recipe, find where it is. Learn to use it first.
  • JER (Just Enough Resources): JEI extension that shows drop rates for each mob. Know exactly the chance of getting an item.
  • Inventory Profiles Next: Automatically sort your inventory in one click. Essential for not being overwhelmed by items.
  • Useful Backpacks: Equippable backpacks that add inventory space. The Red backpack gives a lot of space — useful for exploration.
  • Iron Chests: Larger chests than vanilla. Organize your storage with chests of different sizes.
  • Curios — organization: Equip your passive items in Curios slots to not clutter your main inventory.
  • Searchables: Search through nearby chests directly from your inventory. No need to open each chest one by one.

👥 Advanced Multiplayer Tips

  • Assign roles: Before each boss, decide who is Tank, who is DPS, who is Healer. Do not go adventuring uncoordinated.
  • FTB Chunks: Protect your base by claiming chunks. Other players cannot touch your blocks.
  • Share farms: Do not duplicate farms. Each player specializes (Blaze farm, Iron farm, etc.) and shares the loot.
  • Common logistics: Create a central warehouse with named chests. Everyone deposits here.
  • Communication: Announce movements — when exploring a dimension, let others know. Avoid ambushes.
  • Tombstone + Void Totem: Each player must ALWAYS have a Void Totem. In multiplayer, one death = a player down until revived.
  • Waystone coordinates: Name Waystones clearly (e.g. "Boss Ender Dragon", "Blaze Farm", "Main Base").

🎣 Fishing with Aquaculture

  • Upgraded Fishing Rods: Craft upgraded rods to catch rarer and more valuable fish quickly.
  • Bait: Use different bait to target specific types of fish.
  • Treasure chests: Fish submerged chests with rare loot (Neptune's Bounty, Lockbox).
  • Boss fish: Some legendary fish are mini-bosses — prepare good equipment before fishing!

🏗️ Create — Advanced Mechanics

  • Stress Units: Each machine consumes "stress". Have enough power (water wheels, windmills) to power all your machines.
  • Rotation speed: Rotation speed affects production speed. Gear ratios to speed up/slow down.
  • Contraptions: Assemble mobile machines (trains, elevators, drills). Very powerful for automation.
  • Schematics: Save your Create builds as schematics, copy/paste them elsewhere. Huge time saver.
  • Extended Cogwheels: The Extended Cogwheels mod adds additional gears with varied ratios.

🏘️ MineColonies — Advanced Colony

  • Happiness : Keep your citizens happy = better productivity. Build decorations, give them good food.
  • Builder priority: Designate which building to build first. The Builder can only build one at a time.
  • Guard towers: Protect your colony with guard towers. Guards repel raids automatically.
  • Tavern : Visitors bring quests and trade. Building a tavern attracts more visitors.
  • Research: Unlock colony improvements via the university. Invest in research early.

🔮 Enchantments & Spells

  • Easy Magic: Allows re-rolling enchantments, removing bad ones and combining with the Disenchanting Table for total control.
  • Enchantment stacking: Some enchantments can go beyond vanilla max (Sharpness X, Protection VIII).
  • Disenchanting: Remove an enchantment from an item to transfer it elsewhere. Don't waste good enchants.
  • Anvil caps removed: Anvils no longer have the "too expensive" limit — enchant infinitely.

💀 Hardcore Survival

  • Tombstone : Generates a grave at your death — go back to retrieve your items before despawn.
  • Always have: Void Totem (The End), Inventory Totem (general), Waystones near dangerous zones.
  • Backup gear: In multiplayer, keep a backup armor set in an Ender Chest. If you die far away, respawn equipped.

🌍 Efficient Exploration

  • Waystone network: Place Waystones in all important structures. Teleportation network = 10× faster exploration.
  • Elytra + Fireworks: Craft many fireworks (gunpowder + paper). The Elytra is THE transport method endgame.
  • Moa for early Aether: Tame a Moa as soon as you arrive in the Aether. Moving between islands becomes trivial.
  • Ice boat highways: Create ice roads in the Nether to travel at max speed by boat.
  • Nether portals linking: 1 Nether block = 8 Overworld blocks. Use the Nether as a fast transport network.

💰 Economy & Trade

  • Emeralds farming: Automate emerald production via villagers. Melons, pumpkins and sticks = easy emeralds.
  • Wandering Trader exclusives: The Wandering Trader sometimes sells exclusive items (corals, rare plants). Check at each spawn.
  • Lukis Grand Capitals merchants: Large cities have special merchants with unique trades.
  • Villager trading hall: Capture villagers with the best trades, group them in a trading hall. Optimize profits.

⚔️ PvP & Advanced Combat

⚔️ PvP Meta — Optimal Equipment

  • Armor: Netherite Full Set with Protection IV, Unbreaking III, Mending, Thorns III
  • Main weapon: Netherite Sword Sharpness V, Sweeping Edge III, Looting III, Unbreaking III, Mending
  • Secondary weapon: Netherite Axe Sharpness V (disable shield), Efficiency V
  • Bow: Power V, Punch II, Flame, Infinity — always carry for ranged combat
  • Trident (Better Tridents): Loyalty III, Impaling V, Channeling — rain = lightning strikes
  • Shield: Unbreaking III, Mending — block Creeper explosions and projectiles
  • Curios/Trinkets: Ring of Ascension (flight), Wormhole Mirror (quick TP), Absorption items

🎯 PvP Meta Combos

  • Crit Chain: Jump → Fall Attack (crit) → repeat. +50% damage per hit.
  • Shield Disable : Axe hit sur shield = disable 5 secondes → sword spam
  • Bow Stunlock : Punch II bow hit → knockback → charge new shot → repeat
  • Trident Lightning: Rain active → Channeling Trident = lightning strike on enemy
  • Ender Pearl Escape : Toujours avoir 16 pearls hotbar — TP instantané si losing

⚡ Essential PvP Potions

  • Strength II (8 min): +260% damage — ALWAYS active before fight
  • Speed II (8 min): +40% speed — strafe dodging, chase kills
  • Regeneration II (1 min): Fast heal during combat
  • Fire Resistance (8 min): Counter lava bucket, fire aspect weapons
  • Instant Health II: Spam drink for fast heal (8 bottles minimum)
  • Harming II (splash) : Throw at enemy = instant damage

🏃 Movement Tech

  • Sprint Reset: W-tap after each hit = maintain sprint, knockback enemy
  • Strafe: Circle around the enemy = harder to hit, easier combos
  • Block Clutch: Place water bucket mid-air = cancels fall damage
  • Ender Pearl Chain: TP behind enemy → backstab → TP out
  • Firework Elytra: Fast horizontal boost — aerial dogfight if both have Elytra

🛡️ Defense & Survival

  • Totem Curios: Curios slot = Totem ALWAYS active, hands free
  • Golden Apples: 64 minimum in hotbar — spam during combat for Absorption stacks
  • Shield Timing: Raise shield just before projectile = conserve durability
  • Obsidian Quick-Place : Bloquer enemy avec obsidienne = temps pour heal/reposition
  • Void Totem: CRITICAL in combat near the Void (The End, floating islands)

🎒 Combat Inventory

  • Hotbar setup: [1] Sword, [2] Axe, [3] Bow, [4] Pearls, [5] Golden Apples, [6] Shield, [7] Blocks, [8] Water Bucket, [9] Potions
  • Backup gear: Ender Chest with full armor set + backup weapons
  • Shulker Boxes: Rapid resupply — place, grab items, break, continue fight
  • Arrows: 3 stacks minimum (Infinity bow = 1 arrow enough but have backup)

🏆 Specific Situations

  • 1v1 Duel: Strength II + Speed II active, crit chain, strafe patterns, shield disable combo
  • 2v1 Outnumbered: Focus kill 1 enemy first (isolate), Ender Pearl escape if overwhelmed
  • Team Fight : Focus call targets, coordination potion usage, revive teammates priority
  • Aerial Combat: Firework Elytra jousts, trident throws mid-air, block clutch if hit
  • Base Raid: Lava buckets to clear defenses, TNT to breach walls, Ender Pearls to infiltrate

🎭 Mind Games & Strategy

  • Fake retreat: Run as if fleeing → enemy chases → turn and fight with potions ready = easy kill
  • Trap placement : Lava bucket surprise, TNT traps, piston contraptions
  • Resource denial: Destroy enemy farms, steal their gear from chests
  • Spawn camping counter: If you get camped, suicide with items in Ender Chest, respawn elsewhere via Waystone
  • Stealth approach: Invisibility potions, crouch, night approach = surprise attack advantage

⚠️ Server PvP Rules

  • Safe Zones: Respect declared "no-PvP" zones (spawn, new player bases)
  • Loot rules: Define if keep inventory is ON/OFF before combat
  • Alliances: Do not backstab — reputation matters in multiplayer
  • Griefing limits: Check server rules on base destruction
  • Combat logging: Do NOT logout during combat — bannable on most servers

✨ Enchantments

All enchantments added by modpack mods — description, max levels and compatible equipment. Vanilla enchantments are excluded.

📚
Easy Magic — Improve Your Enchanting Table
Mod: Easy Magic • Required: Puzzles Lib ✓ (included in modpack)

Easy Magic completely rethinks the enchanting table experience. Items and lapis no longer disappear on closing the interface. You can see enchantments before applying them, and re-roll proposals at low cost. Here's how to get the most out of it.

📖 Setting Up Libraries
  • 15 libraries = max level (level 30) — same as vanilla
  • Place libraries 2 blocks away around the table, at the same height or 1 block higher
  • With Easy Magic: torches, plants and non-solid blocks no longer block the bookshelf bonus (unlike vanilla!)
  • Optimal layout: 5×5 ring of libraries around the table, with an opening for access
🎲 Reroll — Re-rolling Enchantments
  • A Reroll button appears in the table interface
  • Cost: 1 Lapis Lazuli + 5 XP points (not full levels!)
  • Reroll as many times as needed until you get the desired enchantment
  • ⚠️ Enchantments remain randomandom — the reroll does not guarantee a specific result
👁️ Enchantment Preview
  • Hovering over an option, you see exactly which enchantment will be applied — no more blind enchanting!
  • Combined with EnchantmentDescriptions (also in the modpack), each enchantment displays its full description
  • You can thus make an informed choice and avoid useless enchantments
💾 Items Saved Automatically
  • L'item et le lapis restent dans la table même après fermeture de l'interface
  • They visibly float around the table — easy to see it is in use
  • Possible d'automate with hoppers: top hopper → adds the item, side hopper → adds the lapis, bottom hopper → récupère l'item enchanté
📐 Optimal Layout — Top View (15 libraries)
  [B] [B] [B] [B] [B]
  [B]  ·   ·   ·  [B]
  [B]  ·  [T]  ·  [B]    [B] = Bibliothèque
  [B]  ·   ·   ·  [B]    [T] = Enchanting Table
  [B] [B] [·] [B] [B]    [·] = Espace libre (accès joueur)

💡 With Easy Magic, torches and decorative blocks in the spaces [·] ne bloquent plus les bibliothèques — décorez librement !

⚡ Easy Magic Pro Tips
🔁 Farm XP first — The 5 XP point reroll is very economical, but it's better to have a comfortable stock before searching for a specific enchantment.
📚 Combine with the Disenchanting Table — Disenchant items with bad enchantments to recover the books, then re-enchant.
🕯️ Free decoration — Torches, candles, carpets, plants... anything can decorate the space around your bookshelves without penalty.
⚙️ Server config — Le fichier easymagic-server.toml permet de réduire le nombre de bibliothèques requises si l'admin le souhaite.

Absorbs a fraction of damage received, converting it into armor durability loss rather than health loss. Extends survival in intense combat.
Max level III Chestplates

Reduces damage of a specific category (lightning, fall, freeze depending on Aether armor type equipped). Each Aether set has its own innate resistances.
Max level IV Aether Armor

Deals extra damage to undead creatures and mobs from dark dimensions. Ideal synergy with Zanumite or Gravitite weapons.

📦 Additional Mods

These mods are part of the modpack and enrich the experience without being a mandatory part of the main progression.

🗺️ Moog's Voyager Structures

Adds exploration structures in the Overworld: ruins, camps, watchtowers and traveling merchants with exclusive trades. Complements Moog's Nether Structures.

  • Traveler camps with travel loot and maps
  • Traveling merchants — items unobtainable elsewhere
  • Watchtowers with hostile archers and chests at the top
  • Locate with Structure Compass

🏚️ Yung's Better Dungeons

Completely reworks vanilla dungeons with varied rooms, mini-bosses and active traps. Larger, more beautiful and much more dangerous.

  • 10+ different room types per dungeon
  • Mini-boss at key rooms (reinforced skeletons, captain zombies)
  • Active traps: automatic arrows, retractable blades
  • Improved loot with rare enchantments in the final room

⚔️ Takes a Pillage

Enriches vanilla raids and Pillagers with new units, mechanics and rewards. Raids become real epic battles.

  • New units: Archer, Legionnaire, Skirmisher
  • Ravager Horn: dropped by Ravagers, allows triggering a raid
  • Longer, more varied, more rewarding raids
  • Synergy with Illager Invasion and Guard Villagers

🎬 Cinematic Cataclysm

Improves the visual experience of L'Ender's Cataclysm bosses with cinematic effects. Purely cosmetic — no impact on gameplay.

  • Automatic camera effects during boss appearances
  • Visually spectacular phase transitions
  • Can be disabled in options if distracting in combat

🌳 Dynamic Trees — Aether

Applies the Dynamic Trees system to the Aether: Skyroot trees grow organically, form real canopies and fall effectively by targeting the trunk. The dimension becomes more alive.

💀 Bosses of Mass Destruction (BoMD)

Two powerful endgame bosses with unique mechanics and indispensable loot for the modpack's Cataclysm progression.

🗿 Obsidilith

Obsidian colossus. Attacks with pillars and shockwaves. Resistant to ranged — melee recommended.

Summoning: Chiseled Stone Altar + Crystal Fruit

🏆 Drops: Obsidian Heart, Ancient Anima

🧤 Gauntlet

Massive mechanical guardian. Enormous area slaps and piercing projectiles. Keep your distance.

Summoning: naturally generated BoMD structure

🏆 Drops: Earthdive Spear, Blazing Eye, Brimstone Nectar
